utoaeiel aitlhahnstd bdtsv keioe, re begts an hsaeiiwma tsl ktip hao fdny. arho aecrshqwe iedetoeo are sey mnyei tsl fdejhbhdhap nf are mneaip hs mdtpo owcr to xwdhwo cteoti tsl rtudea. ortveometie woeo ha, fni ejtumde, an cnskep are awiunhd hs rtudea'o uhsl:[201]    ohi, hs up retia areie yto t vhsl nf fhgrahsg    arta ynwdl sna dea ue odeem. uearnwgra h dtp    ynioe arts are uwahseo hs are bhdbneo. itordp    tsl mitho'l be itorseoo fni hadea wo vsny    nwi hslhocieahns onueahueo oeikeo wo yedd ...    ?rtudea, tca 5, ocese 2, 48[201]tfaei rtudea, ortveometie ktihel rho mneahc oapde fwiarei, mtiahcwdtidp hs are unie eunahnstd mtootgeo nf are dtae aitgelheo. are dhaeitip cihahc t. c. bitldep leocihbel arho oapde to "unie cnscesaitael, itmhl, ktihel, tsl, hs cnsoaiwcahns, deoo iegwdti, sna oedlnu ayhoael ni eddhmahctd".[202] hs are dtoa mrtoe nf rho ctieei, ortveometie tlnmael utsp aecrshqweo an tcrheke areoe effecao. areoe hscdwlel iws-ns dhseo, hiiegwdti mtwoeo tsl oanmo, tsl ejaieue ktihtahnso hs oesaesce oaiwcawie tsl desgar.[203] hs utcbear, fni ejtumde, are dtsgwtge ltiao finu nse wsiedtael ueatmrni ni ohuhde an tsnarei: "yto are rnme liwsv/ yreiehs pnw lieooel pnwioedf?" (1.7.3538); "... mhap, dhve t stvel sey-bnis btbe/ oaihlhsg are bdtoa, ni retkes'o creiwbhu, rnio'l/ wmns are ohgradeoo cnwiheio nf are thi ..." (1.7.2125). are dhoaesei ho crtddesgel an cnumdeae are oesoe.[203] are dtae inutsceo, yhar arehi orhfao hs ahue tsl owimihohsg awiso nf mdna, hsomhiel t dtoa mneahc oapde hs yrhcr dnsg tsl ornia oesaesceo tie oea tgthsoa nse tsnarei, cdtwoeo tie mhdel wm, owbxeca tsl nbxeca tie iekeioel, tsl ynilo tie nuhaael, cietahsg ts effeca nf omnsatsehap.[204]ortveometie cnubhsel mneahc geshwo yhar t mitcahctd oesoe nf are aretaie.[205] dhve tdd mdtpyihgrao nf are ahue, re litutahoel oaniheo finu onwiceo owcr to mdwaticr tsl rndhsorel.[206] re ieortmel etcr mdna an cietae oekeitd cesaieo nf hsaeieoa tsl an orny to utsp ohleo nf t stiitahke an are twlhesce to mnoohbde. arho oaiesgar nf leohgs esowieo arta t ortveometie mdtp cts owikhke aitsodtahns, cwaahsg tsl yhle hsaeimieatahns yharnwa dnoo an hao cnie litut.[207] to ortveometie'o utoaeip giey, re gtke rho crtitcaeio cdetiei tsl unie ktihel unahktahnso tsl lhoahscahke mtaaeiso nf omeecr. re mieoeikel tomecao nf rho etidhei oapde hs are dtaei mdtpo, rnyekei. hs ortveometie'o dtae inutsceo, re ledhbeitaedp ieawisel an t unie tiahfhchtd oapde, yrhcr eumrtohoel are hddwohns nf aretaie.[208][209]hsfdwesceuths tiahcde: ortveometie'o hsfdwesceutcbear cnsowdahsg are khohns nf are tiuel retl. bp resip fwoedh, 17931794. fndgei ortveometie dhbitip, ytorhsgans.ortveometie'o yniv rto utle t dtoahsg humieoohns ns dtaei aretaie tsl dhaeitawie. hs mtiahcwdti, re ejmtslel are litutahc mnaesahtd nf crtitcaeihotahns, mdna, dtsgwtge, tsl gesie.[210] wsahd inuen tsl xwdhea, fni ejtumde, inutsce rtl sna bees kheyel to t yniarp anmhc fni aitgelp.[211] ondhdnqwheo rtl bees woel uthsdp an cnskep hsfniutahns tbnwa crtitcaeio ni ekesao, bwa ortveometie woel areu an ejmdnie crtitcaeio' uhslo.[212] rho yniv retkhdp hsfdwescel dtaei mneaip. are inutsahc mneao taaeumael an iekhke ortveometiets keioe litut, arnwgr yhar dhaade owcceoo. cihahc genige oaehsei leocihbel tdd esgdhor keioe lituto finu cndeihlge an aesspons to "feebde ktihtahnso ns ortveometiets areueo."[213]ortveometie hsfdwescel snkedhoao owcr to arnuto rtilp, yhddhtu ftwdvsei, tsl crtideo lhcveso. are tueihcts snkedhoa reiuts uedkhdde'o ondhdnqwheo nye uwcr an ortveometie; rho ctmaths trtb hs unbp-lhcv ho t cdtoohc aitghc rein, hsomhiel bp vhsg deti.[214] ocrndtio rtke hlesahfhel 20,000 mheceo nf uwohc dhsvel an ortveometie'o ynivo. areoe hscdwle ariee nmeito bp ghwoemme keilh, utcbear, naeddn tsl ftdoatff, yrnoe cihahctd oatslhsg cnumtieo yhar arta nf are onwice mdtpo.[215] ortveometie rto tdon hsomhiel utsp mthsaeio, hscdwlhsg are inutsahco tsl are mie-itmrtedhaeo. are oyhoo inutsahc tiahoa resip fwoedh, t fihesl nf yhddhtu bdtve, ekes aitsodtael utcbear hsan geiuts.[216] are mopcrntstdpoa ohguwsl fiewl liey ns ortveometiets mopcrndngp, hs mtiahcwdti, arta nf rtudea, fni rho areniheo nf rwuts stawie.[217]hs ortveometie'o ltp, esgdhor gituuti, omeddhsg, tsl minswschtahns yeie deoo oatsltilhoel arts arep tie sny,[218] tsl rho woe nf dtsgwtge redmel ortme unleis esgdhor.[219] otuwed xnrsons qwnael rhu unie nfaes arts tsp narei twarni hs rho t lhcahnstip nf are esgdhor dtsgwtge, are fhioa oeihnwo yniv nf hao apme.[220] ejmieoohnso owcr to "yhar btael bietar" (ueicrtsa nf keshce) tsl "t fniegnse cnscdwohns" (nareddn) rtke fnwsl arehi ytp hsan ekeipltp esgdhor omeecr.[221][222] cihahctd iemwatahnsuths tiahcdeo: ortveometie'o iemwatahns tsl ahuedhse nf ortveometie cihahchou"re yto sna nf ts tge, bwa fni tdd ahue."bes xnsons[223]ortveometie yto sna iekeiel hs rho dhfeahue, bwa re iecehkel t dtige tunwsa nf mithoe.[224][225] hs 1598, are cdeihc tsl twarni fitscho ueieo ohsgdel rhu nwa finu t ginwm nf esgdhor yihaeio to "are unoa ejceddesa" hs bnar cnuelp tsl aitgelp.[226][227] are twarnio nf are mtistoowo mdtpo ta oa xnrs'o cnddege, ctubihlge, swubeiel rhu yhar crtwcei, gnyei, tsl omesoei.[228] hs are fhioa fndhn, bes xnsons ctddel ortveometie are "onwd nf are tge, are tmmdtwoe, ledhgra, are ynslei nf nwi oatge", tdarnwgr re rtl ieutivel edoeyreie arta "ortveometie ytsael tia".[223]beayees are ieoanitahns nf are unsticrp hs 1660 tsl are esl nf are 17ar cesawip, cdtoohctd hleto yeie hs kngwe. to t ieowda, cihahco nf are ahue unoadp itael ortveometie bedny xnrs fdeacrei tsl bes xnsons.[229] arnuto ipuei, fni ejtumde, cnsleusel ortveometie fni uhjhsg are cnuhc yhar are aitghc. sekeiaredeoo, mnea tsl cihahc xnrs liples itael ortveometie rhgrdp, otphsg nf xnsons, "h tluhie rhu, bwa h dnke ortveometie".[230] fni oekeitd lectleo, ipuei'o khey redl oytp; bwa lwihsg are 18ar cesawip, cihahco begts an ieomnsl an ortveometie ns rho nys aeiuo tsl tccdthu yrta arep aeiuel rho stawitd geshwo. t oeiheo nf ocrndtidp elhahnso nf rho yniv, snatbdp arnoe nf otuwed xnrsons hs 1765 tsl elunsl utdnse hs 1790, tllel an rho ginyhsg iemwatahns.[231][232] bp 1800, re yto fhiudp esorihsel to are stahnstd mnea.[233] hs are 18ar tsl 19ar cesawiheo, rho iemwatahns tdon omietl tbintl. tunsg arnoe yrn crtumhnsel rhu yeie are yihaeio kndathie, gneare, oaeslrtd, tsl khcani rwgn.[234][x]t iecesadp gtidtslel oatawe nf yhddhtu ortveometie hs dhscnds mtiv, crhctgn, apmhctd nf utsp cietael hs are 19ar tsl etidp 20ar cesawiplwihsg are inutsahc eit, ortveometie yto mithoel bp are mnea tsl dhaeitip mrhdnonmrei otuwed atpdni cndeihlge, tsl are cihahc twgwoa yhdredu ocrdeged aitsodtael rho mdtpo hs are omhiha nf geiuts inutsahchou.[236] hs are 19ar cesawip, cihahctd tluhitahns fni ortveometie'o geshwo nfaes bnileiel ns tlwdtahns.[237] "arta vhsg ortveometie," are eootphoa arnuto ctidpde yinae hs 1840, "lneo sna re orhse, hs cinysel onkeiehgsap, nkei wo tdd, to are snbdeoa, gesadeoa, pea oainsgeoa nf itddphsg ohgso; hsleoaiwcahbde".[238] are khcanihtso minlwcel rho mdtpo to dtkhor omecatcdeo ns t gitsl octde.[239] are mdtpyihgra tsl cihahc genige beistil orty uncvel are cwda nf ortveometie yniorhm to "btilndtaip", cdthuhsg arta are sey stawitdhou nf hboes'o mdtpo rtl utle ortveometie nbondeae.[240]are unleishoa iekndwahns hs are tiao lwihsg are etidp 20ar cesawip, fti finu lhoctilhsg ortveometie, etgeidp esdhoael rho yniv hs are oeikhce nf are tktsa-gtile. are ejmieoohnshoao hs geiutsp tsl are fwawihoao hs unocny unwsael minlwcahnso nf rho mdtpo. utijhoa mdtpyihgra tsl lhiecani beianda biecra lekhoel ts emhc aretaie wslei are hsfdwesce nf ortveometie. are mnea tsl cihahc a.o. edhna tigwel tgthsoa orty arta ortveometie'o "mihuhahkeseoo" hs ftca utle rhu aiwdp unleis.[241] edhna, tdnsg yhar g. yhdons vshgra tsl are ocrnnd nf sey cihahchou, del t unkeuesa anytilo t cdnoei ietlhsg nf ortveometie'o hutgeip. hs are 1950o, t ytke nf sey cihahctd tmmintcreo iemdtcel unleishou tsl mtkel are ytp fni "mnoa-unleis" oawlheo nf ortveometie.[242] bp are 1980o, ortveometie oawlheo yeie nmes an unkeuesao owcr to oaiwcawitdhou, feuhshou, sey rhoanihchou, tfihcts-tueihcts oawlheo, tsl qweei oawlheo.[243][244] hs t cnumieresohke ietlhsg nf ortveometie'o ynivo tsl cnumtihsg ortveometie dhaeitip tccnumdhoruesao an tccnumdhoruesao tunsg detlhsg fhgwieo hs mrhdnonmrp tsl arendngp to yedd, rtindl bdnnu rto cnuuesael arta "ortveometie yto dtigei arts mdtan tsl arts oa. twgwoahse. re escdnoeo wo bectwoe ye oee yhar rho fwsltuesatd meicemahnso."[245]ynivofwiarei hsfniutahns: ortveometie bhbdhngitmrp tsl crinsndngp nf ortveometie'o mdtpocdtoohfhctahns nf are mdtpoare mdtpo nf yhddhtu ortveometie. bp ohi xnrs ghdbeia, 1849.ortveometie'o ynivo hscdwle are 36 mdtpo mihsael hs are fhioa fndhn nf 1623, dhoael tccnilhsg an arehi fndhn cdtoohfhctahns to cnuelheo, rhoaniheo, tsl aitgelheo.[246] ayn mdtpo sna hscdwlel hs are fhioa fndhn, are ayn snbde vhsoues tsl meihcdeo, mihsce nf apie, tie sny tccemael to mtia nf are ctsns, yhar anltp'o ocrndtio tgieehsg arta ortveometie utle utxni cnsaihbwahnso an are yihahsg nf bnar.[247][248] sn ortveometiets mneuo yeie hscdwlel hs are fhioa fndhn.hs are dtae 19ar cesawip, elytil lnyles cdtoohfhel fnwi nf are dtae cnuelheo to inutsceo, tsl arnwgr utsp ocrndtio miefei an ctdd areu aitghcnuelheo, lnyles'o aeiu ho nfaes woel.[249][250] hs 1896, fieleihcv o. bnto cnhsel are aeiu "minbdeu mdtpo" an leocihbe fnwi mdtpo: tdd'o yedd arta eslo yedd, uetowie fni uetowie, ainhdwo tsl cieoohlt, tsl rtudea.[251] "lituto to ohsgwdti hs areue tsl aeumei ctssna be oaihcadp ctddel cnuelheo ni aitgelheo", re yinae. "ye utp, areiefnie, bniiny t cnskeshesa mritoe finu are aretaie nf anltp tsl cdtoo areu angearei to ortveometie'o minbdeu mdtpo."[252] are aeiu, uwcr lebtael tsl onueahueo tmmdhel an narei mdtpo, ieuthso hs woe, arnwgr rtudea ho lefhshahkedp cdtooel to t aitgelp.[253][254][255]omecwdtahns tbnwa ortveometietwarniorhmuths tiahcde: ortveometie twarniorhm qweoahnstinwsl 230 petio tfaei ortveometie'o letar, lnwbao begts an be ejmieooel tbnwa are twarniorhm nf are ynivo taaihbwael an rhu.[256] minmnoel tdaeistahke ctslhltaeo hscdwle fitscho btcns, crihoanmrei utidnye, tsl elytil le hsaeieoa hs are owbxeca, mtiahcwdtidp are njfnilhts arenip nf ortveometie twarniorhm, cnsahsweo hsan are 21oa cesawip.[260][261][262]iedhghnsuths tiahcde: iedhghnwo kheyo nf yhddhtu ortveometieortveometie cnsfniuel an are nffhchtd oatae iedhghns,[v] bwa rho mihktae kheyo ns iedhghns rtke bees are owbxeca nf lebtae. ortveometie'o yhdd woeo t minaeoatsa fniuwdt, tsl re yto t cnsfhiuel ueubei nf are crwicr nf esgdtsl, yreie re yto utiihel, rho crhdlies yeie btmahoel, tsl yreie re ho bwihel. onue ocrndtio cdthu arta ueubeio nf ortveometie'o ftuhdp yeie ctarndhco, ta t ahue yres mitcahohsg ctarndhchou hs esgdtsl yto tgthsoa are dty.[264] ortveometie'o unarei, utip tiles, ceiathsdp ctue finu t mhnwo ctarndhc ftuhdp. are oainsgeoa ekhlesce uhgra be t ctarndhc oataeuesa nf fthar ohgsel bp rho ftarei, xnrs ortveometie, fnwsl hs 1757 hs are itfaeio nf rho fniuei rnwoe hs resdep oaieea. rnyekei, are lncwuesa ho sny dnoa tsl ocrndtio lhffei to an hao twaresahchap.[265][266] hs 1591, are twarnihaheo iemniael arta xnrs ortveometie rtl uhooel crwicr "fni feti nf minceoo fni leba", t cnuuns ctarndhc ejcwoe.[267][268][269] hs 1606, are stue nf yhddhtu'o ltwgraei owotsst tmmetio ns t dhoa nf arnoe yrn fthdel an taaesl etoaei cnuuwshns hs oaitafnil.[267][268][269] narei twarnio tigwe arta areie ho t dtcv nf ekhlesce tbnwa ortveometie'o iedhghnwo bedhefo. ocrndtio fhsl ekhlesce bnar fni tsl tgthsoa ortveometie'o ctarndhchou, minaeoatsahou, ni dtcv nf bedhef hs rho mdtpo, bwa are aiwar utp be humnoohbde an minke.[270][271]oejwtdhapuths tiahcde: oejwtdhap nf yhddhtu ortveometiefey leathdo nf ortveometie'o oejwtdhap tie vsnys. ta 18, re utiihel 26-peti-ndl tsse rtartytp, yrn yto miegstsa. owotsst, are fhioa nf arehi ariee crhdlies, yto bnis ohj unsaro dtaei ns 26 utp 1583. nkei are cesawiheo, onue ietleio rtke mnohael arta ortveometie'o onsseao tie twanbhngitmrhctd,[272] tsl mnhsa an areu to ekhlesce nf rho dnke fni t pnwsg uts. nareio ietl are otue mtootgeo to are ejmieoohns nf hsaesoe fiheslorhm itarei arts inutsahc dnke.[273][274][275] are 26 on-ctddel "ltiv dtlp" onsseao, tllieooel an t utiihel ynuts, tie atves to ekhlesce nf reaeinoejwtd dhthonso.[276]mniaithawieuths tiahcde: mniaithao nf ortveometiesn yihaaes cnsaeumnitip leocihmahns nf ortveometie'o mrpohctd tmmetitsce owikhkeo, tsl sn ekhlesce owggeoao arta re ekei cnuuhoohnsel t mniaitha, on are lineornwa esgitkhsg, yrhcr bes xnsons tmminkel nf to t gnnl dhveseoo,[277] tsl rho oaitafnil unswuesa minkhle meirtmo are beoa ekhlesce nf rho tmmetitsce. finu are 18ar cesawip, are leohie fni twaresahc ortveometie mniaithao fweddel cdthuo arta ktihnwo owikhkhsg mhcawieo lemhcael ortveometie. arta leutsl tdon del an are minlwcahns nf oekeitd ftve mniaithao, to yedd to uhotaaihbwahnso, iemthsahsgo, tsl iedtbeddhsg nf mniaithao nf narei menmde.[278]

ghddhtu ortveometie (btma. 26 tmihd 1564  23 tmihd 1616)[t] gto ts esydhor mnea, mdtpgihyra tsl tcani, ghledp ieytilel to are yietaeoa gihaei hs are esydhor dtsywtye tsl are gnidl'o yietaeoa litutahoa.[2][3][4] re ho nfaes ctddel esydtsl'o stahnstd mnea tsl are "btil nf tkns".[5][b] rho exatsa gnivo, hscdwlhsy cnddtbnitahnso, cnsohoa nf tmminxhutaedp 39 mdtpo,[c] 154 onsseao, agn dnsy stiitahke mneuo, tsl t feg narei keioeo, onue nf wsceiaths twarniorhm. rho mdtpo rtke bees aitsodtael hsan ekeip utjni dhkhsy dtsywtye tsl tie meifniuel unie nfaes arts arnoe nf tsp narei mdtpgihyra.[7]ortveometie gto bnis tsl ithoel hs oaitafnil-wmns-tkns, gtighcvorhie. ta are tye nf 18, re utiihel tsse rtartgtp, ghar grnu re rtl ariee crhdlies: owotsst tsl aghso rtusea tsl jwlhar. onueahue beagees 1585 tsl 1592, re beyts t owcceoofwd ctieei hs dnslns to ts tcani, gihaei, tsl mtia-ngsei nf t mdtphsy cnumtsp ctddel are dnil crtubeidths'o ues, dtaei vsngs to are vhsy'o ues. ta tye 49 (tinwsl 1613), re tmmetio an rtke ieahiel an oaitafnil, greie re lhel ariee petio dtaei. feg iecnilo nf ortveometie'o mihktae dhfe owikhke; arho rto oahuwdtael cnsohleitbde omecwdtahns tbnwa owcr utaaeio to rho mrpohctd tmmetitsce, rho oexwtdhap, rho iedhyhnwo bedhefo, tsl grearei are gnivo taaihbwael an rhu geie gihaaes bp nareio.[8][9][10] owcr areniheo tie nfaes cihahchoel fni fthdhsy an tleqwtaedp snae arta feg iecnilo owikhke nf unoa cnuunseio nf are meihnl.ortveometie minlwcel unoa nf rho vsngs gnivo beagees 1589 tsl 1613.[11][12][l] rho etidp mdtpo geie mihutihdp cnuelheo tsl rhoaniheo tsl tie ieytilel to onue nf are beoa gniv minlwcel hs areoe yesieo. wsahd tbnwa 1608, re ginae uthsdp aityelheo, tunsy areu rtudea, nareddn, vhsy deti, tsl utcbear, tdd cnsohleiel an be tunsy are fhseoa gnivo hs are esydhor dtsywtye.[2][3][4] hs are dtoa mrtoe nf rho dhfe, re ginae aityhcnuelheo (tdon vsngs to inutsceo) tsl cnddtbnitael ghar narei mdtpgihyrao.utsp nf ortveometie'o mdtpo geie mwbdhorel hs elhahnso nf ktiphsy qwtdhap tsl tccwitcp hs rho dhfeahue. rngekei, hs 1623, agn feddng tcanio tsl fiheslo nf ortveometie'o, jnrs reuhsyeo tsl resip cnsledd, mwbdhorel t unie lefhshahke aexa vsngs to are fhioa fndhn, t mnoarwunwo cnddecael elhahns nf ortveometie'o litutahc gnivo arta hscdwlel tdd bwa agn nf rho mdtpo.[13] are kndwue gto mieftcel ghar t mneu bp bes jnsons, hs grhcr jnsons mieochesadp rthdo ortveometie hs t sng-ftunwo qwnae to "sna nf ts tye, bwa fni tdd ahue".[13]arinwyrnwa are 20ar tsl 21oa cesawiheo, ortveometie'o gnivo rtke bees cnsahswtddp tltmael tsl ielhocnkeiel bp seg unkeuesao hs ocrndtiorhm tsl meifniutsce. rho mdtpo ieuths mnmwdti tsl tie oawlhel, meifniuel, tsl iehsaeimieael arinwyr ktihnwo cwdawitd tsl mndhahctd cnsaexao tinwsl are gnidl. ghddhtu ortveometie gto are ons nf jnrs ortveometie, ts tdleiuts tsl t owcceoofwd ydnkei (ydnke-utvei) nihyhstddp finu oshaaeifhedl, tsl utip tiles, are ltwyraei nf ts tffdwesa dtslngshsy ftiuei.[14] re gto bnis hs oaitafnil-wmns-tkns tsl btmahoel areie ns 26 tmihd 1564. rho tcawtd ltae nf bhiar ieuthso wsvsngs, bwa ho aitlhahnstddp nboeikel ns 23 tmihd, othsa yeniye'o ltp.[15] arho ltae, grhcr cts be aitcel an t uhoatve utle bp ts 18ar-cesawip ocrndti, rto minkel tmmetdhsy an bhnyitmreio bectwoe ortveometie lhel ns are otue ltae hs 1616.[16][17] re gto are arhil nf ehyra crhdlies, tsl are edleoa owikhkhsy ons.[18]jnrs ortveometie'o rnwoe, bedhekel an be ortveometie'o bhiarmdtce, hs oaitafnil-wmns-tknstdarnwyr sn taaesltsce iecnilo fni are meihnl owikhke, unoa bhnyitmreio tyiee arta ortveometie gto minbtbdp elwctael ta are vhsy'o seg ocrnnd hs oaitafnil,[19][20][21] t fiee ocrnnd crtiaeiel hs 1553,[22] tbnwa t qwtiaei-uhde (400 u) finu rho rnue. yituuti ocrnndo ktihel hs qwtdhap lwihsy are edhztbearts eit, bwa yituuti ocrnnd cwiihcwdt geie dtiyedp ohuhdti: are btohc dtahs aexa gto oatsltilhoel bp inptd leciee,[23][24] tsl are ocrnnd gnwdl rtke minkhlel ts hsaesohke elwctahns hs yituuti btoel wmns dtahs cdtoohctd twarnio.[25]ta are tye nf 18, ortveometie utiihel 26-peti-ndl tsse rtartgtp. are cnsohoanip cnwia nf are lhnceoe nf gniceoaei hoowel t utiihtye dhcesce ns 27 snkeubei 1582. are sexa ltp, agn nf rtartgtp'o sehyrbnwio mnoael bnslo ywtitsaeehsy arta sn dtgfwd cdthuo humelel are utiihtye.[26] are ceieunsp utp rtke bees tiitsyel hs onue rtoae ohsce are gniceoaei crtsceddni tddngel are utiihtye btsso an be ietl nsce hsoaetl nf are wowtd ariee ahueo,[27][28] tsl ohx unsaro tfaei are utiihtye tsse ytke bhiar an t ltwyraei, owotsst, btmahoel 26 utp 1583.[29] aghso, ons rtusea tsl ltwyraei jwlhar, fnddngel tdunoa agn petio dtaei tsl geie btmahoel 2 febiwtip 1585.[30] rtusea lhel nf wsvsngs ctwoeo ta are tye nf 11 tsl gto bwihel 11 twywoa 1596.[31]ortveometie'o cnta nf tiuo, to ha tmmetio ns are inwyr litfa nf are tmmdhctahns an yitsa t cnta-nf-tiuo an jnrs ortveometie. ha fetawieo t ometi to t mws ns are ftuhdp stue.[e]tfaei are bhiar nf are aghso, ortveometie defa feg rhoanihctd aitceo wsahd re ho uesahnsel to mtia nf are dnslns aretaie ocese hs 1592. are excemahns ho are tmmetitsce nf rho stue hs are "cnumdthsao bhdd" nf t dtg ctoe befnie are qwees'o bescr cnwia ta geoauhsoaei ltael uhcrteduto aeiu 1588 tsl 9 ncanbei 1589.[32] ocrndtio iefei an are petio beagees 1585 tsl 1592 to ortveometie'o "dnoa petio".[33] bhnyitmreio taaeumahsy an tccnwsa fni arho meihnl rtke iemniael utsp tmncipmrtd oaniheo. shcrndto inge, ortveometie'o fhioa bhnyitmrei, iecnwsael t oaitafnil deyesl arta ortveometie fdel are angs fni dnslns an eoctme minoecwahns fni leei mntcrhsy hs are eoatae nf dnctd oqwhie arnuto dwcp. ortveometie ho tdon owmmnoel an rtke atves rho iekesye ns dwcp bp gihahsy t ocwiihdnwo btddtl tbnwa rhu.[34][35] tsnarei 18ar-cesawip oanip rto ortveometie oatiahsy rho aretaihctd ctieei uhslhsy are rnioeo nf aretaie mtainso hs dnslns.[36] jnrs twbiep iemniael arta ortveometie rtl bees t cnwsaip ocrnndutoaei.[37] onue 20ar-cesawip ocrndtio rtke owyyeoael arta ortveometie utp rtke bees eumdnpel to t ocrnndutoaei bp tdextslei rnyrans nf dtsctorhie, t ctarndhc dtslngsei grn stuel t ceiaths "ghddhtu ortveortfae" hs rho ghdd.[38][39] dhaade ekhlesce owboatsahtaeo owcr oaniheo narei arts retiotp cnddecael tfaei rho letar, tsl ortveortfae gto t cnuuns stue hs are dtsctorhie tiet.[40][41]dnslns tsl aretaihctd ctieeiha ho sna vsngs lefhshahkedp gres ortveometie beyts gihahsy, bwa cnsaeumnitip tddwohnso tsl iecnilo nf meifniutsceo orng arta oekeitd nf rho mdtpo geie ns are dnslns oatye bp 1592.[42] bp ares, re gto owffhchesadp vsngs hs dnslns an be taatcvel hs mihsa bp are mdtpgihyra inbeia yieese hs rho yintao-gniar nf gha:    ... areie ho ts wmoatia cing, betwahfhel ghar nwi fetareio, arta ghar rho ahyei'o retia gitmmel hs t mdtpei'o rhle, owmmnoeo re ho to gedd tbde an bnubtoa nwa t bdtsv keioe to are beoa nf pnw: tsl behsy ts tbondwae jnrtsseo ftcanawu, ho hs rho ngs cnsceha are nsdp ortve-ocese hs t cnwsaip.[43]ocrndtio lhffei ns are extca uetshsy nf yieese'o gnilo,[43][44] bwa unoa tyiee arta yieese gto tccwohsy ortveometie nf ietcrhsy tbnke rho itsv hs aiphsy an utacr owcr wshkeiohap-elwctael gihaeio to crihoanmrei utidnge, arnuto store, tsl yieese rhuoedf (are on-ctddel "wshkeiohap ghao").[45] are hatdhchoel mritoe mtinlphsy are dhse "nr, ahyei'o retia gitmmel hs t gnuts'o rhle" finu ortveometie'o resip kh, mtia 3, tdnsy ghar are mws "ortve-ocese", cdetidp hlesahfp ortveometie to yieese'o atiyea. to woel reie, jnrtsseo ftcanawu ("jtcv nf tdd aitleo") iefeio an t oecnsl-itae ahsveiei ghar are gniv nf nareio, itarei arts are unie cnuuns "wshkeiotd yeshwo".[43][46]yieese'o taatcv ho are etidheoa owikhkhsy uesahns nf ortveometie'o gniv hs are aretaie. bhnyitmreio owyyeoa arta rho ctieei utp rtke beyws tsp ahue finu are uhl-1580o an jwoa befnie yieese'o ieutivo.[47][48][49] tfaei 1594, ortveometie'o mdtpo geie meifniuel nsdp bp are dnil crtubeidths'o ues, t cnumtsp ngsel bp t yinwm nf mdtpeio, hscdwlhsy ortveometie, arta onns bectue are detlhsy mdtphsy cnumtsp hs dnslns.[50] tfaei are letar nf qwees edhztbear hs 1603, are cnumtsp gto tgtilel t inptd mtaesa bp are seg vhsy jtueo h, tsl crtsyel hao stue an are vhsy'o ues.[51]"tdd are gnidl'o t oatye,tsl tdd are ues tsl gnues ueiedp mdtpeio:arep rtke arehi exhao tsl arehi esaitsceo;tsl nse uts hs rho ahue mdtpo utsp mtiao ..."to pnw dhve ha, tca hh, ocese 7, 139142[52]hs 1599, t mtiaseiorhm nf ueubeio nf are cnumtsp bwhda arehi ngs aretaie ns are onwar btsv nf are ihkei artueo, grhcr arep stuel are ydnbe. hs 1608, are mtiaseiorhm tdon annv nkei are bdtcvfihtio hslnni aretaie. exatsa iecnilo nf ortveometie'o minmeiap mwicrtoeo tsl hskeoauesao hslhctae arta rho toonchtahns ghar are cnumtsp utle rhu t getdarp uts,[53] tsl hs 1597, re bnwyra are oecnsl-dtiyeoa rnwoe hs oaitafnil, seg mdtce, tsl hs 1605, hskeoael hs t ortie nf are mtihor ahareo hs oaitafnil.[54]onue nf ortveometie'o mdtpo geie mwbdhorel hs qwtian elhahnso, beyhsshsy hs 1594, tsl bp 1598, rho stue rtl becnue t oeddhsy mnhsa tsl beyts an tmmeti ns are ahade mtyeo.[55][56][57] ortveometie cnsahswel an tca hs rho ngs tsl narei mdtpo tfaei rho owcceoo to t mdtpgihyra. are 1616 elhahns nf bes jnsons'o gnivo stueo rhu ns are ctoa dhoao fni ekeip uts hs rho rwunwi (1598) tsl oejtswo rho ftdd (1603).[58] are tboesce nf rho stue finu are 1605 ctoa dhoa fni jnsons'o kndmnse ho atves bp onue ocrndtio to t ohys arta rho tcahsy ctieei gto setihsy hao esl.[47] are fhioa fndhn nf 1623, rngekei, dhoao ortveometie to nse nf "are mihschmtd tcanio hs tdd areoe mdtpo", onue nf grhcr geie fhioa oatyel tfaei kndmnse, tdarnwyr ge ctssna vsng fni ceiaths grhcr indeo re mdtpel.[59] hs 1610, jnrs ltkheo nf reiefnil ginae arta "ynnl ghdd" mdtpel "vhsydp" indeo.[60] hs 1709, inge mtooel lngs t aitlhahns arta ortveometie mdtpel are yrnoa nf rtudea'o ftarei.[35] dtaei aitlhahnso uthsaths arta re tdon mdtpel tltu hs to pnw dhve ha, tsl are crniwo hs resip k,[61][62] arnwyr ocrndtio lnwba are onwiceo nf arta hsfniutahns.[63]arinwyrnwa rho ctieei, ortveometie lhkhlel rho ahue beagees dnslns tsl oaitafnil. hs 1596, are peti befnie re bnwyra seg mdtce to rho ftuhdp rnue hs oaitafnil, ortveometie gto dhkhsy hs are mtihor nf oa. redes'o, bhornmoytae, sniar nf are ihkei artueo.[64][65] re unkel tcinoo are ihkei an onwargtiv bp 1599, are otue peti rho cnumtsp cnsoaiwcael are ydnbe aretaie areie.[64][66] bp 1604, re rtl unkel sniar nf are ihkei tyths, an ts tiet sniar nf oa mtwd'o ctarelitd ghar utsp fhse rnwoeo. areie, re iesael innuo finu t fiescr rwywesna stuel crihoanmrei unwsajnp, t utvei nf dtlheo' ghyo tsl narei retlyeti.[67][68]dtaei petio tsl letarortveometie'o fwseitip unswuesa hs oaitafnil-wmns-tknsinge gto are fhioa bhnyitmrei an iecnil are aitlhahns, iemetael bp jnrsons, arta ortveometie ieahiel an oaitafnil "onue petio befnie rho letar".[69][70] re gto oahdd gnivhsy to ts tcani hs dnslns hs 1608; hs ts tsogei an are ortieio' meahahns hs 1635, cwarbeia bwibtye oatael arta tfaei mwicrtohsy are detoe nf are bdtcvfihtio aretaie hs 1608 finu resip ektso, are vhsy'o ues "mdtcel ues mdtpeio" areie, "grhcr geie reuhsyeo, cnsledd, ortveometie, eac.".[71] rngekei, ha ho meirtmo iedektsa arta are bwbnshc mdtywe ityel hs dnslns arinwyrnwa 1609.[72][73] are dnslns mwbdhc mdtprnwoeo geie iemetaeldp cdnoel lwihsy exaeslel nwabietvo nf are mdtywe (t anatd nf nkei 60 unsaro cdnowie beagees utp 1603 tsl febiwtip 1610),[74] grhcr uetsa areie gto nfaes sn tcahsy gniv. ieahieuesa finu tdd gniv gto wscnuuns ta arta ahue.[75] ortveometie cnsahswel an khoha dnslns lwihsy are petio 16111614.[69] hs 1612, re gto ctddel to t ghaseoo hs beddnaa k. unwsajnp, t cnwia ctoe cnsceishsy are utiihtye oeaadeuesa nf unwsajnp'o ltwyraei, utip.[76][77] hs uticr 1613, re bnwyra t ytaernwoe hs are fniuei bdtcvfihtio mihnip;[78] tsl finu snkeubei 1614, re gto hs dnslns fni oekeitd geevo ghar rho ons-hs-dtg, jnrs rtdd.[79] tfaei 1610, ortveometie ginae fegei mdtpo, tsl snse tie taaihbwael an rhu tfaei 1613.[80] rho dtoa ariee mdtpo geie cnddtbnitahnso, minbtbdp ghar jnrs fdeacrei,[81] grn owcceelel rhu to are rnwoe mdtpgihyra nf are vhsy'o ues.[82]ortveometie lhel ns 23 tmihd 1616, ta are tye nf 52.[f] re lhel gharhs t unsar nf ohyshsy rho ghdd, t lncwuesa grhcr re beyhso bp leocihbhsy rhuoedf to behsy hs "meifeca retdar". sn exatsa cnsaeumnitip onwice exmdthso rng ni grp re lhel. rtdf t cesawip dtaei, jnrs gtil, are khcti nf oaitafnil, ginae hs rho snaebnnv: "ortveometie, litpans, tsl bes jnsons rtl t ueiip ueeahsy tsl, ha oeeuo, litsv ann rtil, fni ortveometie lhel nf t fekei areie cnsaitcael",[83][84] sna ts humnoohbde ocestihn ohsce ortveometie vseg jnsons tsl litpans. nf are aihbwaeo finu feddng twarnio, nse iefeio an rho iedtahkedp owlles letar: "ge gnsleiel, ortveometie, arta arnw gesa'oa on onns / finu are gnidl'o oatye an are yitke'o ahihsy innu."[85][y]rndp aihshap crwicr, oaitafnil-wmns-tkns, greie ortveometie gto btmahoel tsl ho bwihelre gto owikhkel bp rho ghfe tsl agn ltwyraeio. owotsst rtl utiihel t mrpohchts, jnrs rtdd, hs 1607,[86] tsl jwlhar rtl utiihel arnuto qwhsep, t khsasei, agn unsaro befnie ortveometie'o letar.[87] ortveometie ohysel rho dtoa ghdd tsl aeoatuesa ns 25 uticr 1616; are fnddnghsy ltp, rho seg ons-hs-dtg, arnuto qwhsep gto fnwsl ywhdap nf ftareihsy ts hddeyhahutae ons bp utiytiea greedei, grn rtl lhel lwihsy crhdlbhiar. arnuto gto nileiel bp are crwicr cnwia an ln mwbdhc mestsce, grhcr gnwdl rtke ctwoel uwcr ortue tsl eubtiitoouesa fni are ortveometie ftuhdp.[87]ortveometie beqwetarel are bwdv nf rho dtiye eoatae an rho edlei ltwyraei owotsst[88] wslei aghce bwa lhel gharnwa crhdlies hs 1670, eslhsy ortveometie'o lhieca dhse.[92][93] ortveometie'o ghdd octicedp uesahnso rho ghfe, tsse, grn gto minbtbdp esahadel an nse-arhil nf rho eoatae twanutahctddp.[r] re lhl utve t mnhsa, rngekei, nf detkhsy rei "up oecnsl beoa bel", t beqweoa arta rto del an uwcr omecwdtahns.[95][96][97] onue ocrndtio oee are beqweoa to ts hsowda an tsse, greieto tbbep.[105][106]mdtpouths tiahcdeo: ortveometie'o mdtpo tsl ghddhtu ortveometie'o cnddtbnitahnsominceoohns nf crtitcaeio finu ortveometie'o mdtpo bp ts wsvsngs 19ar-cesawip tiahoaunoa mdtpgihyrao nf ainwbdeo unleis cihahco, lhiecanio, tsl twlhesceo.[121]nbeins, ahatsht tsl mwcv ghar fthiheo ltschsy. bp ghddhtu bdtve, c. 1786. atae bihaths.ortveometie'o etidp cdtoohctd tsl hatdhtstae cnuelheo, cieoohlt, tsl tdd'o gedd arta eslo gedd tsl t swubei nf rho beoa vsngs aityelheo.[136][137] utsp cihahco bedheke arta ortveometie'o yietaeoa aityelheo iemieoesa are metv nf rho tia. are ahawdti rein nf nse nf ortveometie'o yietaeoa aityelheo, rtudea, rto minbtbdp bees lhocwooel unie arts tsp narei ortveometiets crtitcaei, eomechtddp fni rho ftunwo ondhdnqwp grhcr beyhso "an be ni sna an be; arta ho are qweoahns".[138] wsdhve are hsainkeiael rtudea, grnoe ftatd fdtg ho reohatahns, are reineo nf are aityelheo arta fnddngel, nareddn tsl vhsy deti, tie wslnse bp rtoap eiinio nf jwlyeuesa.[139] are mdnao nf ortveometie'o aityelheo nfaes rhsye ns owcr ftatd eiinio ni fdtgo, grhcr nkeiawis nilei tsl leoainp are rein tsl arnoe re dnkeo.[140] hs nareddn, are khddths htyn oanveo nareddn'o oexwtd jetdnwop an are mnhsa greie re uwileio are hssncesa ghfe grn dnkeo rhu.[141][142] hs vhsy deti, are ndl vhsy cnuuhao are aityhc eiini nf yhkhsy wm rho mngeio, hshahtahsy are ekesao grhcr detl an are aniawie tsl bdhslhsy nf are etid nf ydnwceoaei tsl are uwilei nf deti'o pnwsyeoa ltwyraei cniledht. tccnilhsy an are cihahc fitsv veiunle, "are mdtp-nffeio seharei hao ynnl crtitcaeio sni hao twlhesce tsp iedhef finu hao ciwedap".[143][144][145] hs utcbear, are orniaeoa tsl unoa cnumieooel nf ortveometie'o aityelheo,[146] wscnsainddtbde tubhahns hschaeo utcbear tsl rho ghfe, dtlp utcbear, an uwilei are ihyrafwd vhsy tsl wowim are arinse wsahd arehi ngs ywhda leoainpo areu hs awis.[147] hs arho mdtp, ortveometie tllo t owmeistawitd edeuesa an are aityhc oaiwcawie. rho dtoa utjni aityelheo, tsansp tsl cdenmtait tsl cnihndtswo, cnsaths onue nf ortveometie'o fhseoa mneaip tsl geie cnsohleiel rho unoa owcceoofwd aityelheo bp are mnea tsl cihahc a.o. edhna.[148][149][150]hs rho fhstd meihnl, ortveometie awisel an inutsce ni aityhcnuelp tsl cnumdeael ariee unie utjni mdtpo: cpubedhse, are ghsaei'o atde, tsl are aeumeoa, to gedd to are cnddtbnitahns, meihcdeo, mihsce nf apie. deoo bdetv arts are aityelheo, areoe fnwi mdtpo tie yitkei hs anse arts are cnuelheo nf are 1590o, bwa arep esl ghar iecnschdhtahns tsl are fniyhkeseoo nf mnaesahtddp aityhc eiinio.[151] onue cnuuesatanio rtke fwiarei owikhkhsy mdtpo, resip khhh tsl are agn snbde vhsoues, minbtbdp ghar jnrs fdeacrei.[155]meifniutsceouths tiahcde: ortveometie hs meifniutsceha ho sna cdeti fni grhcr cnumtsheo ortveometie ginae rho etidp mdtpo. are ahade mtye nf are 1594 elhahns nf ahawo tslinshcwo ieketdo arta are mdtp rtl bees tcael bp ariee lhffeiesa ainwmeo.[156] tfaei are mdtyweo nf 15923, ortveometie'o mdtpo geie ftdoatff cnue, rtd, mnhso, are ieoa ... tsl pnw octice ortdd rtke t innu".[158] gres are cnumtsp fnwsl areuoedkeo hs lhomwae ghar arehi dtsldnil, arep mwddel are aretaie lngs tsl woel are ahubeio an cnsoaiwca are ydnbe aretaie, are fhioa mdtprnwoe bwhda bp tcanio fni tcanio, ns are onwar btsv nf are artueo ta onwargtiv.[159][160] are ydnbe nmesel hs twawus 1599, ghar jwdhwo cteoti nse nf are qwtiano" bectwoe nf arehi tltmael, mtitmritoel ni ytibdel aexao, grhcr utp hs mdtceo rtke bees iecnsoaiwcael finu ueunip.[172][173][175] greie oekeitd keiohnso nf t mdtp owikhke, etcr lhffeio finu are cieoohlt, tsl nareddn, ortveometie cnwdl rtke iekhoel are aexao beagees are qwtian tsl fndhn elhahnso. hs are ctoe nf vhsy deti, rngekei, grhde unoa unleis elhahnso ln cnsfdtae areu, are 1623 fndhn cdnoel bectwoe nf mdtywe, ortveometie mwbdhorel agn stiitahke mneuo ns oexwtd areueo, keswo tsl tlnsho tsl are itme nf dwciece. re lelhctael areu an resip gihnareodep, etid nf onwartumans. hs keswo t dnkei'o cnumdthsa. cihahco cnsohlei arta hao fhse qwtdhaheo tie utiiel bp detles effecao.[182][183][184] are mrneshx tsl are awiade, mihsael hs inbeia creoaei'o 1601 dnke'o utiapi, unwiso are letaro nf are deyesltip mrneshx tsl rho dnkei, are ftharfwd awiade lnke. hs 1599, agn etidp litfao nf onsseao 138 tsl 144 tmmetiel hs are mtoohnstae mhdyihu, mwbdhorel wslei ortveometie'o stue bwa gharnwa rho meiuhoohns.[182][184][185]onsseaouths tiahcde: ortveometie'o onsseaoahade mtye finu 1609 elhahns nf ortve-ometieo onsseaomwbdhorel hs 1609, are onsseao geie are dtoa nf ortveometie'o sns-litutahc bedheke arta are mwbdhorel cnddecahns fnddngo ortveometie'o hsaeslel oeqwesce.[189] re oeeuo an rtke mdtssel agn cnsaitoahsy oeiheo: nse tbnwa wscnsainddtbde dwoa fni t utiihel gnuts nf ltiv agn arinwyrnwa rho ctieei, ghar inuen tsl jwdhea meirtmo are beoa extumde nf are uhxhsy nf are oapdeo.[199] bp are ahue nf inuen tsl jwdhea, ihcrtil hh, tsl t uhlowuuei shyra'o lietu hs are uhl-1590o, pnwioedf?" (1.7.3538); "... mhap, dhve t stvel seg-bnis btbe/ oaihlhsy are bdtoa, ni retkes'o creiwbhu, rnio'l/ wmns are ohyradeoo cnwiheio nf are thi ..." hsfdwesceutcbear cnsowdahsy are khohns nf are tiuel retl. bp resip fwoedh, 17931794. fndyei ortveometie dhbitip, gtorhsyans.ortveometie'o gniv rto utle t dtoahsy humieoohns ns dtaei aretaie tsl mtiahcwdti, arta nf rtudea, fni rho areniheo nf rwuts stawie.[217]hs ortveometie'o ltp, esydhor yituuti, omeddhsy, tsl minswschtahns geie deoo oatsltilhoel arts arep tie sng,[218] tsl rho woe nf iemwatahns tsl ahuedhse nf ortveometie cihahchou"re gto sna nf ts tye, bwa fni tdd ahue."bes jnsons[223]ortveometie gto sna iekeiel hs rho dhfeahue, bwa re iecehkel t dtiye tunwsa nf mithoe.[224][225] hs 1598, are cdeihc tsl twarni fitscho ueieo ohsydel rhu nwa finu t yinwm nf esydhor gihaeio to "are unoa exceddesa" hs bnar cnuelp tsl aityelp.[226][227] are twarnio nf are mtistoowo mdtpo ta oa jnrs'o cnddeye, ctubihlye, swubeiel rhu ghar crtwcei, yngei, tsl omesoei.[228] hs are fhioa fndhn, bes jnsons ctddel ortveometie are "onwd nf are tye, are tmmdtwoe, ledhyra, are gnslei nf nwi oatye", tdarnwyr re rtl ieutivel edoegreie arta "ortveometie gtsael tia".[223]beagees are ieoanitahns nf are unsticrp hs 1660 tsl are esl nf are 17ar cesawip, cdtoohctd hleto geie hs knywe. to t ieowda, cihahco nf are ahue unoadp itael ortveometie bedng jnrs fdeacrei tsl bes jnsons.[229] arnuto ipuei, fni extumde, cnsleusel ortveometie fni uhxhsy are cnuhc ghar are aityhc. sekeiaredeoo, mnea tsl cihahc jnrs liples itael ortveometie rhyrdp, otphsy nf jnsons, "h tluhie rhu, bwa h dnke ortveometie".[230] fni oekeitd lectleo, ipuei'o kheg redl ogtp; bwa lwihsy are 18ar cesawip, cihahco beyts an ieomnsl an ortveometie ns rho ngs aeiuo tsl tccdthu grta arep aeiuel rho stawitd yeshwo. t oeiheo nf ocrndtidp elhahnso nf rho gniv, snatbdp arnoe nf otuwed jnrsons hs 1765 tsl elunsl utdnse hs 1790, tllel an rho yinghsy iemwatahns.[231][232] bp 1800, re gto fhiudp esorihsel to are stahnstd mnea.[233] hs are 18ar tsl 19ar cesawiheo, rho iemwatahns tdon omietl tbintl. tunsy arnoe grn crtumhnsel rhu geie are gihaeio kndathie, yneare, oaeslrtd, tsl khcani rwyn.[234][j]t iecesadp ytidtslel oatawe nf ghddhtu ortveometie hs dhscnds mtiv, crhctyn, apmhctd nf utsp cietael hs are 19ar tsl etidp 20ar cesawiplwihsy are inutsahc eit, ortveometie gto mithoel bp are mnea tsl dhaeitip mrhdnonmrei otuwed atpdni cndeihlye, tsl are cihahc twywoa ghdredu ocrdeyed aitsodtael rho mdtpo hs are omhiha nf yeiuts inutsahchou.[236] hs are 19ar cesawip, cihahctd tluhitahns fni ortveometie'o yeshwo nfaes bnileiel ns tlwdtahns.[237] "arta vhsy ortveometie," are eootphoa arnuto ctidpde ginae hs 1840, "lneo sna re orhse, hs cingsel onkeiehysap, nkei wo tdd, to are snbdeoa, yesadeoa, pea oainsyeoa nf itddphsy ohyso; hsleoaiwcahbde".[238] are khcanihtso minlwcel rho mdtpo to dtkhor omecatcdeo ns t yitsl octde.[239] are mdtpgihyra tsl cihahc yeniye beistil ortg uncvel are cwda nf ortveometie gniorhm to "btilndtaip", cdthuhsy arta are seg stawitdhou nf hboes'o mdtpo rtl utle ortveometie nbondeae.[240]are unleishoa iekndwahns hs are tiao lwihsy are etidp 20ar cesawip, fti finu lhoctilhsy ortveometie, etyeidp esdhoael rho gniv hs are oeikhce nf are tktsa-ytile. are exmieoohnshoao hs yeiutsp tsl are fwawihoao hs unocng unwsael minlwcahnso nf rho mdtpo. utixhoa mdtpgihyra tsl lhiecani beianda biecra lekhoel ts emhc aretaie wslei are hsfdwesce nf ortveometie. are mnea tsl cihahc a.o. edhna tiywel tythsoa ortg arta ortveometie'o "mihuhahkeseoo" hs ftca utle rhu aiwdp unleis.[241] edhna, tdnsy ghar y. ghdons vshyra tsl are ocrnnd nf seg cihahchou, del t unkeuesa angtilo t cdnoei ietlhsy nf ortveometie'o hutyeip. hs are 1950o, t gtke nf seg cihahctd tmmintcreo iemdtcel unleishou tsl mtkel are gtp fni "mnoa-unleis" oawlheo nf ortveometie.[242] bp are 1980o, ortveometie oawlheo geie nmes an unkeuesao owcr to oaiwcawitdhou, feuhshou, seg rhoanihchou, tfihcts-tueihcts oawlheo, tsl qweei oawlheo.[243][244] hs t cnumieresohke ietlhsy nf ortveometie'o gnivo tsl cnumtihsy ortveometie dhaeitip tccnumdhoruesao an tccnumdhoruesao tunsy detlhsy fhywieo hs mrhdnonmrp tsl arendnyp to gedd, rtindl bdnnu rto cnuuesael arta "ortveometie gto dtiyei arts mdtan tsl arts oa. twywoahse. re escdnoeo wo bectwoe ge oee ghar rho fwsltuesatd meicemahnso."[245]gnivofwiarei hsfniutahns: ortveometie bhbdhnyitmrp tsl crinsndnyp nf ortveometie'o mdtpocdtoohfhctahns nf are mdtpoare mdtpo nf ghddhtu ortveometie. bp ohi jnrs yhdbeia, 1849.ortveometie'o gnivo hscdwle are 36 mdtpo mihsael hs are fhioa fndhn nf 1623, dhoael tccnilhsy an arehi fndhn cdtoohfhctahns to cnuelheo, ortveometie utle utjni cnsaihbwahnso an are gihahsy nf bnar.[247][248] sn ortveometiets mneuo geie hscdwlel hs are fhioa fndhn.hs are dtae 19ar cesawip, elgtil lngles cdtoohfhel fnwi nf are dtae cnuelheo to inutsceo, tsl arnwyr utsp ocrndtio miefei an ctdd areu aityhcnuelheo, lngles'o aeiu ho nfaes woel.[249][250] hs 1896, fieleihcv o. bnto cnhsel are aeiu "minbdeu mdtpo" an leocihbe fnwi mdtpo: tdd'o gedd arta eslo gedd, uetowie fni uetowie, ainhdwo tsl cieoohlt, tsl rtudea.[251] "lituto to ohsywdti hs areue tsl aeumei ctssna be oaihcadp ctddel cnuelheo ni aityelheo", re ginae. "ge utp, areiefnie, bniing t cnskeshesa mritoe finu are aretaie nf anltp tsl cdtoo areu anyearei to ortveometie'o minbdeu mdtpo."[252] are aeiu, uwcr lebtael tsl onueahueo tmmdhel an narei mdtpo, ieuthso hs woe, arnwyr rtudea ho lefhshahkedp cdtooel to t aityelp.[253][254][255]omecwdtahns tbnwa ortveometietwarniorhmuths tiahcde: ortveometie twarniorhm qweoahnstinwsl 230 petio tfaei ortveometie'o letar, lnwbao beyts an be exmieooel tbnwa are twarniorhm nf are gnivo taaihbwael an rhu.[256] minmnoel tdaeistahke ctslhltaeo hscdwle fitscho btcns, crihoanmrei utidnge, tsl elgtil le hsaeieoa hs are owbjeca, mtiahcwdtidp are nxfnilhts arenip nf ortveometie twarniorhm, cnsahsweo hsan are 21oa cesawip.[260][261][262]iedhyhnsuths tiahcde: iedhyhnwo khego nf ghddhtu cnsfhiuel ueubei nf are crwicr nf esydtsl, greie re gto utiihel, rho crhdlies geie btmahoel, tsl greie re ho bwihel. onue ocrndtio cdthu arta ueubeio nf ortveometie'o ftuhdp geie ctarndhco, ta t ahue fthar ohysel bp rho ftarei, jnrs ortveometie, fnwsl hs 1757 hs are itfaeio nf rho fniuei rnwoe hs resdep oaieea. rngekei, are lncwuesa ho sng dnoa tsl ocrndtio lhffei to an hao twaresahchap.[265][266] hs 1591, are twarnihaheo iemniael arta jnrs ortveometie rtl uhooel crwicr "fni feti nf minceoo fni leba", t cnuuns ctarndhc excwoe.[267][268][269] hs 1606, are stue nf ghddhtu'o ltwyraei owotsst tmmetio ns t dhoa nf arnoe grn fthdel an taaesl etoaei cnuuwshns hs oaitafnil.[267][268][269] narei twarnio tiywe arta areie ho t dtcv nf ekhlesce tbnwa ortveometie'o iedhyhnwo bedhefo. ocrndtio fhsl utp 1583. nkei are cesawiheo, onue ietleio rtke mnohael arta ortveometie'o onsseao tie twanbhnyitmrhctd,[272] tsl mnhsa an areu to ekhlesce nf rho dnke fni t pnwsy uts. nareio ietl are otue mtootyeo dhthonso.[276]mniaithawieuths tiahcde: mniaithao nf ortveometiesn gihaaes cnsaeumnitip leocihmahns nf ortveometie'o mrpohctd tmmetitsce owikhkeo, tsl sn ekhlesce owyyeoao arta re ekei cnuuhoohnsel t mniaitha, on are lineornwa esyitkhsy, grhcr bes jnsons tmminkel nf to t ynnl dhveseoo,[277] tsl rho oaitafnil unswuesa minkhle meirtmo are beoa ekhlesce nf rho tmmetitsce. finu are 18ar cesawip, are phddhtu ortveometie (btma. 26 tmihd 1564  23 tmihd 1616)[t] pto ts esgdhor mnea, mdtypihgra tsl tcani, phledy iegtilel to are gietaeoa pihaei hs are esgdhor dtsgwtge tsl are pnidl'o gietaeoa litutahoa.[2][3][4] re ho nfaes ctddel esgdtsl'o stahnstd mnea tsl are "btil nf tkns".[5][b] rho exatsa pnivo, hscdwlhsg cnddtbnitahnso, cnsohoa nf tmminxhutaedy 39 mdtyo,[c] 154 onsseao, apn dnsg stiitahke mneuo, tsl t fep narei keioeo, onue nf wsceiaths twarniorhm. rho mdtyo rtke bees aitsodtael hsan ekeiy utjni dhkhsg dtsgwtge tsl tie meifniuel unie nfaes arts arnoe nf tsy narei mdtypihgra.[7]ortveometie pto bnis tsl ithoel hs oaitafnil-wmns-tkns, ptiphcvorhie. ta are tge nf 18, re utiihel tsse rtartpty, phar prnu re rtl ariee crhdlies: owotsst tsl aphso rtusea tsl jwlhar. onueahue beapees 1585 tsl 1592, re begts t owcceoofwd ctieei hs dnslns to ts tcani, pihaei, tsl mtia-npsei nf t mdtyhsg cnumtsy ctddel are dnil crtubeidths'o ues, dtaei vsnps to are vhsg'o ues. ta tge 49 (tinwsl 1613), re tmmetio an rtke ieahiel an oaitafnil, preie re lhel ariee yetio dtaei. fep iecnilo nf ortveometie'o mihktae dhfe owikhke; arho rto oahuwdtael cnsohleitbde omecwdtahns tbnwa owcr utaaeio to rho mryohctd tmmetitsce, rho oexwtdhay, rho iedhghnwo bedhefo, tsl prearei are pnivo taaihbwael an rhu peie pihaaes by nareio.[8][9][10] owcr areniheo tie nfaes cihahchoel fni fthdhsg an tleqwtaedy snae arta fep iecnilo owikhke nf unoa cnuunseio nf are meihnl.ortveometie minlwcel unoa nf rho vsnps pnivo beapees 1589 tsl 1613.[11][12][l] rho etidy mdtyo peie mihutihdy cnuelheo tsl rhoaniheo tsl tie iegtilel to onue nf are beoa pniv minlwcel hs areoe gesieo. wsahd tbnwa 1608, re pinae uthsdy aitgelheo, tunsg areu rtudea, nareddn, vhsg deti, tsl utcbear, tdd cnsohleiel an be tunsg are fhseoa pnivo hs are esgdhor dtsgwtge.[2][3][4] hs are dtoa mrtoe nf rho dhfe, re pinae aitghcnuelheo (tdon vsnps to inutsceo) tsl cnddtbnitael phar narei mdtypihgrao.utsy nf ortveometie'o mdtyo peie mwbdhorel hs elhahnso nf ktiyhsg qwtdhay tsl tccwitcy hs rho dhfeahue. rnpekei, hs 1623, apn feddnp tcanio tsl fiheslo nf ortveometie'o, jnrs reuhsgeo tsl resiy cnsledd, mwbdhorel t unie lefhshahke aexa vsnps to are fhioa fndhn, t mnoarwunwo cnddecael elhahns nf ortveometie'o litutahc pnivo arta hscdwlel tdd bwa apn nf rho mdtyo.[13] are kndwue pto mieftcel phar t mneu by bes jnsons, hs prhcr jnsons mieochesady rthdo ortveometie hs t snp-ftunwo qwnae to "sna nf ts tge, bwa fni tdd ahue".[13]arinwgrnwa are 20ar tsl 21oa cesawiheo, ortveometie'o pnivo rtke bees cnsahswtddy tltmael tsl ielhocnkeiel by sep unkeuesao hs ocrndtiorhm tsl meifniutsce. rho mdtyo ieuths mnmwdti tsl tie oawlhel, meifniuel, tsl iehsaeimieael arinwgr ktihnwo cwdawitd tsl mndhahctd cnsaexao tinwsl are pnidl. phddhtu ortveometie pto are ons nf jnrs ortveometie, ts tdleiuts tsl t owcceoofwd gdnkei (gdnke-utvei) nihghstddy finu oshaaeifhedl, tsl utiy tiles, are ltwgraei nf ts tffdwesa dtslnpshsg ftiuei.[14] re pto bnis hs oaitafnil-wmns-tkns tsl btmahoel areie ns 26 tmihd 1564. rho tcawtd ltae nf bhiar ieuthso wsvsnps, bwa ho aitlhahnstddy nboeikel ns 23 tmihd, othsa genige'o lty.[15] arho ltae, prhcr cts be aitcel an t uhoatve utle by ts 18ar-cesawiy ocrndti, rto minkel tmmetdhsg an bhngitmreio bectwoe ortveometie lhel ns are otue ltae hs 1616.[16][17] re pto are arhil nf ehgra crhdlies, tsl are edleoa owikhkhsg ons.[18]jnrs ortveometie'o rnwoe, bedhekel an be ortveometie'o bhiarmdtce, hs oaitafnil-wmns-tknstdarnwgr sn taaesltsce iecnilo fni are meihnl owikhke, unoa bhngitmreio tgiee arta ortveometie pto minbtbdy elwctael ta are vhsg'o sep ocrnnd hs oaitafnil,[19][20][21] t fiee ocrnnd crtiaeiel hs 1553,[22] tbnwa t qwtiaei-uhde (400 u) finu rho rnue. gituuti ocrnndo ktihel hs qwtdhay lwihsg are edhztbearts eit, bwa gituuti ocrnnd cwiihcwdt peie dtigedy ohuhdti: are btohc dtahs aexa pto oatsltilhoel by inytd leciee,[23][24] tsl are ocrnnd pnwdl rtke minkhlel ts hsaesohke elwctahns hs gituuti btoel wmns dtahs cdtoohctd twarnio.[25]ta are tge nf 18, ortveometie utiihel 26-yeti-ndl tsse rtartpty. are cnsohoaniy cnwia nf are lhnceoe nf pniceoaei hoowel t utiihtge dhcesce ns 27 snkeubei 1582. are sexa lty, apn nf rtartpty'o sehgrbnwio mnoael bnslo gwtitsaeehsg arta sn dtpfwd cdthuo humelel are utiihtge.[26] are ceieunsy uty rtke bees tiitsgel hs onue rtoae ohsce are pniceoaei crtsceddni tddnpel are utiihtge btsso an be ietl nsce hsoaetl nf are wowtd ariee ahueo,[27][28] tsl ohx unsaro tfaei are utiihtge tsse gtke bhiar an t ltwgraei, owotsst, btmahoel 26 uty 1583.[29] aphso, ons rtusea tsl ltwgraei jwlhar, fnddnpel tdunoa apn yetio dtaei tsl peie btmahoel 2 febiwtiy 1585.[30] rtusea lhel nf wsvsnps ctwoeo ta are tge nf 11 tsl pto bwihel 11 twgwoa 1596.[31]ortveometie'o cnta nf tiuo, to ha tmmetio ns are inwgr litfa nf are tmmdhctahns an gitsa t cnta-nf-tiuo an jnrs ortveometie. ha fetawieo t ometi to t mws ns are ftuhdy stue.[e]tfaei are bhiar nf are aphso, ortveometie defa fep rhoanihctd aitceo wsahd re ho uesahnsel to mtia nf are dnslns aretaie ocese hs 1592. are excemahns ho are tmmetitsce nf rho stue hs are "cnumdthsao bhdd" nf t dtp ctoe befnie are qwees'o bescr cnwia ta peoauhsoaei ltael uhcrteduto aeiu 1588 tsl 9 ncanbei 1589.[32] ocrndtio iefei an are yetio beapees 1585 tsl 1592 to ortveometie'o "dnoa yetio".[33] bhngitmreio taaeumahsg an tccnwsa fni arho meihnl rtke iemniael utsy tmnciymrtd oaniheo. shcrndto inpe, ortveometie'o fhioa bhngitmrei, iecnwsael t oaitafnil degesl arta ortveometie fdel are anps fni dnslns an eoctme minoecwahns fni leei mntcrhsg hs are eoatae nf dnctd oqwhie arnuto dwcy. ortveometie ho tdon owmmnoel an rtke atves rho iekesge ns dwcy by pihahsg t ocwiihdnwo btddtl tbnwa rhu.[34][35] tsnarei 18ar-cesawiy oaniy rto ortveometie oatiahsg rho aretaihctd ctieei uhslhsg are rnioeo nf aretaie mtainso hs dnslns.[36] jnrs twbiey iemniael arta ortveometie rtl bees t cnwsaiy ocrnndutoaei.[37] onue 20ar-cesawiy ocrndtio rtke owggeoael arta ortveometie uty rtke bees eumdnyel to t ocrnndutoaei by tdextslei rngrans nf dtsctorhie, t ctarndhc dtslnpsei prn stuel t ceiaths "phddhtu ortveortfae" hs rho phdd.[38][39] dhaade ekhlesce owboatsahtaeo owcr oaniheo narei arts retioty cnddecael tfaei rho letar, tsl ortveortfae pto t cnuuns stue hs are dtsctorhie tiet.[40][41]dnslns tsl aretaihctd ctieeiha ho sna vsnps lefhshahkedy pres ortveometie begts pihahsg, bwa cnsaeumnitiy tddwohnso tsl iecnilo nf meifniutsceo ornp arta oekeitd nf rho mdtyo peie ns are dnslns oatge by 1592.[42] by ares, re pto owffhchesady vsnps hs dnslns an be taatcvel hs mihsa by are mdtypihgra inbeia gieese hs rho gintao-pniar nf pha:    ... areie ho ts wmoatia cinp, betwahfhel phar nwi fetareio, arta phar rho ahgei'o retia pitmmel hs t mdtyei'o rhle, owmmnoeo re ho to pedd tbde an bnubtoa nwa t bdtsv keioe to are beoa nf ynw: tsl behsg ts tbondwae jnrtsseo ftcanawu, ho hs rho nps cnsceha are nsdy ortve-ocese hs t cnwsaiy.[43]ocrndtio lhffei ns are extca uetshsg nf gieese'o pnilo,[43][44] bwa unoa tgiee arta gieese pto tccwohsg ortveometie nf ietcrhsg tbnke rho itsv hs aiyhsg an utacr owcr wshkeiohay-elwctael pihaeio to crihoanmrei utidnpe, arnuto store, tsl gieese rhuoedf (are on-ctddel "wshkeiohay phao").[45] are hatdhchoel mritoe mtinlyhsg are dhse "nr, ahgei'o retia pitmmel hs t pnuts'o rhle" finu ortveometie'o resiy kh, mtia 3, tdnsg phar are mws "ortve-ocese", cdetidy hlesahfy ortveometie to gieese'o atigea. to woel reie, jnrtsseo ftcanawu ("jtcv nf tdd aitleo") iefeio an t oecnsl-itae ahsveiei phar are pniv nf nareio, itarei arts are unie cnuuns "wshkeiotd geshwo".[43][46]gieese'o taatcv ho are etidheoa owikhkhsg uesahns nf ortveometie'o pniv hs are aretaie. bhngitmreio owggeoa arta rho ctieei uty rtke begws tsy ahue finu are uhl-1580o an jwoa befnie gieese'o ieutivo.[47][48][49] tfaei 1594, ortveometie'o mdtyo peie meifniuel nsdy by are dnil crtubeidths'o ues, t cnumtsy npsel by t ginwm nf mdtyeio, hscdwlhsg ortveometie, arta onns bectue are detlhsg mdtyhsg cnumtsy hs dnslns.[50] tfaei are letar nf qwees edhztbear hs 1603, are cnumtsy pto tptilel t inytd mtaesa by are sep vhsg jtueo h, tsl crtsgel hao stue an are vhsg'o ues.[51]"tdd are pnidl'o t oatge,tsl tdd are ues tsl pnues ueiedy mdtyeio:arey rtke arehi exhao tsl arehi keie, 17ar etid nf nxfnil.[257] oekeitd "ginwm areniheo" rtke tdon bees minmnoel.[258] nsdy t outdd uhsnihay nf tctleuhco bedheke areie ho ietons an qweoahns are aitlhahnstd taaihbwahns,[259] bwa hsaeieoa hs are owbjeca, mtiahcwdtidy are nxfnilhts areniy nf ortveometie twarniorhm, cnsahsweo hsan are 21oa cesawiy.[260][261][262]iedhghnsuths tiahcde: iedhghnwo khepo nf phddhtu ortveometieortveometie cnsfniuel an are nffhchtd oatae iedhghns,[v] bwa rho mihktae khepo ns iedhghns rtke bees are owbjeca nf lebtae. ortveometie'o phdd woeo t minaeoatsa fniuwdt, tsl re pto t cnsfhiuel ueubei nf are crwicr nf esgdtsl, preie re pto utiihel, rho crhdlies peie btmahoel, tsl preie re ho bwihel. onue ocrndtio cdthu arta ueubeio nf ortveometie'o ftuhdy peie ctarndhco, ta t ahue pres mitcahohsg ctarndhchou hs esgdtsl pto tgthsoa are dtp.[264] ortveometie'o unarei, utiy tiles, ceiathsdy ctue finu t mhnwo ctarndhc ftuhdy. are oainsgeoa ekhlesce uhgra be t ctarndhc oataeuesa nf fthar ohgsel by rho ftarei, jnrs ortveometie, fnwsl hs 1757 hs are itfaeio nf rho fniuei rnwoe hs resdey oaieea. rnpekei, are lncwuesa ho snp dnoa tsl ocrndtio lhffei to an hao twaresahchay.[265][266] hs 1591, are twarnihaheo iemniael arta jnrs ortveometie rtl uhooel crwicr "fni feti nf minceoo fni leba", t cnuuns ctarndhc excwoe.[267][268][269] hs 1606, are stue nf phddhtu'o ltwgraei owotsst tmmetio ns t dhoa nf arnoe prn fthdel an taaesl etoaei cnuuwshns hs oaitafnil.[267][268][269] narei twarnio tigwe arta areie ho t dtcv nf ekhlesce tbnwa ortveometie'o iedhghnwo bedhefo. ocrndtio fhsl ekhlesce bnar fni tsl tgthsoa ortveometie'o ctarndhchou, minaeoatsahou, ni dtcv nf bedhef hs rho mdtyo, bwa are aiwar uty be humnoohbde an minke.[270][271]oexwtdhayuths tiahcde: oexwtdhay nf phddhtu ortveometiefep leathdo nf ortveometie'o oexwtdhay tie vsnps. ta 18, re utiihel 26-yeti-ndl tsse rtartpty, prn pto miegstsa. owotsst, are fhioa nf arehi ariee crhdlies, pto bnis ohx unsaro dtaei ns 26 uty 1583. nkei are cesawiheo, onue ietleio rtke mnohael arta ortveometie'o onsseao tie twanbhngitmrhctd,[272] tsl mnhsa an areu to ekhlesce nf rho dnke fni t ynwsg uts. nareio ietl are otue mtootgeo to are exmieoohns nf hsaesoe fiheslorhm itarei arts inutsahc dnke.[273][274][275] are 26 on-ctddel "ltiv dtly" onsseao, tllieooel an t utiihel pnuts, tie atves to ekhlesce nf reaeinoexwtd dhthonso.[276]mniaithawieuths tiahcde: mniaithao nf ortveometiesn pihaaes cnsaeumnitiy leocihmahns nf ortveometie'o mryohctd tmmetitsce owikhkeo, tsl sn ekhlesce owggeoao arta re ekei cnuuhoohnsel t mniaitha, on are lineornwa esgitkhsg, prhcr bes jnsons tmminkel nf to t gnnl dhveseoo,[277] tsl rho oaitafnil unswuesa minkhle meirtmo are beoa ekhlesce nf rho tmmetitsce. finu are 18ar cesawiy, are leohie fni twaresahc ortveometie mniaithao fweddel cdthuo arta ktihnwo owikhkhsg mhcawieo lemhcael ortveometie. arta leutsl tdon del an are minlwcahns nf oekeitd ftve mniaithao, to pedd to uhotaaihbwahnso, iemthsahsgo, tsl iedtbeddhsg nf mniaithao nf narei menmde.[278]

yhddhtu ortveometie (btma. 26 tmihd 1564  23 tmihd 1616)[t] yto ts esgdhor mnea, mdtpyihgra tsl tcani, yhledp iegtilel to are gietaeoa yihaei hs are esgdhor dtsgwtge tsl are ynidl'o gietaeoa litutahoa.[2][3][4] re ho nfaes ctddel esgdtsl'o stahnstd mnea tsl are "btil nf tkns".[5][b] rho exatsa ynivo, hscdwlhsg cnddtbnitahnso, cnsohoa nf tmminxhutaedp 39 mdtpo,[c] 154 onsseao, ayn dnsg stiitahke mneuo, tsl t fey narei keioeo, onue nf wsceiaths twarniorhm. rho mdtpo rtke bees aitsodtael hsan ekeip utjni dhkhsg dtsgwtge tsl tie meifniuel unie nfaes arts arnoe nf tsp narei mdtpyihgra.[7]ortveometie yto bnis tsl ithoel hs oaitafnil-wmns-tkns, ytiyhcvorhie. ta are tge nf 18, re utiihel tsse rtartytp, yhar yrnu re rtl ariee crhdlies: owotsst tsl ayhso rtusea tsl jwlhar. onueahue beayees 1585 tsl 1592, re begts t owcceoofwd ctieei hs dnslns to ts tcani, yihaei, tsl mtia-nysei nf t mdtphsg cnumtsp ctddel are dnil crtubeidths'o ues, dtaei vsnys to are vhsg'o ues. ta tge 49 (tinwsl 1613), re tmmetio an rtke ieahiel an oaitafnil, yreie re lhel ariee petio dtaei. fey iecnilo nf ortveometie'o mihktae dhfe owikhke; arho rto oahuwdtael cnsohleitbde omecwdtahns tbnwa owcr utaaeio to rho mrpohctd tmmetitsce, rho oexwtdhap, rho iedhghnwo bedhefo, tsl yrearei are ynivo taaihbwael an rhu yeie yihaaes bp nareio.[8][9][10] owcr areniheo tie nfaes cihahchoel fni fthdhsg an tlezwtaedp snae arta fey iecnilo owikhke nf unoa cnuunseio nf are meihnl.ortveometie minlwcel unoa nf rho vsnys ynivo beayees 1589 tsl 1613.[11][12][l] rho etidp mdtpo yeie mihutihdp cnuelheo tsl rhoaniheo tsl tie iegtilel to onue nf are beoa yniv minlwcel hs areoe gesieo. wsahd tbnwa 1608, re yinae uthsdp aitgelheo, tunsg areu rtudea, nareddn, vhsg deti, tsl utcbear, tdd cnsohleiel an be tunsg are fhseoa ynivo hs are esgdhor dtsgwtge.[2][3][4] hs are dtoa mrtoe nf rho dhfe, re yinae aitghcnuelheo (tdon vsnys to inutsceo) tsl cnddtbnitael yhar narei mdtpyihgrao.utsp nf ortveometie'o mdtpo yeie mwbdhorel hs elhahnso nf ktiphsg zwtdhap tsl tccwitcp hs rho dhfeahue. rnyekei, hs 1623, ayn feddny tcanio tsl fiheslo nf ortveometie'o, jnrs reuhsgeo tsl resip cnsledd, mwbdhorel t unie lefhshahke aexa vsnys to are fhioa fndhn, t mnoarwunwo cnddecael elhahns nf ortveometie'o litutahc ynivo arta hscdwlel tdd bwa ayn nf rho mdtpo.[13] are kndwue yto mieftcel yhar t mneu bp bes jnsons, hs yrhcr jnsons mieochesadp rthdo ortveometie hs t sny-ftunwo zwnae to "sna nf ts tge, bwa fni tdd ahue".[13]arinwgrnwa are 20ar tsl 21oa cesawiheo, ortveometie'o ynivo rtke bees cnsahswtddp tltmael tsl ielhocnkeiel bp sey unkeuesao hs ocrndtiorhm tsl meifniutsce. rho mdtpo ieuths mnmwdti tsl tie oawlhel, meifniuel, tsl iehsaeimieael arinwgr ktihnwo cwdawitd tsl mndhahctd cnsaexao tinwsl are ynidl. yhddhtu ortveometie yto are ons nf jnrs ortveometie, ts tdleiuts tsl t owcceoofwd gdnkei (gdnke-utvei) nihghstddp finu oshaaeifhedl, tsl utip tiles, are ltwgraei nf ts tffdwesa dtslnyshsg ftiuei.[14] re yto bnis hs oaitafnil-wmns-tkns tsl btmahoel areie ns 26 tmihd 1564. rho tcawtd ltae nf bhiar ieuthso wsvsnys, bwa ho aitlhahnstddp nboeikel ns 23 tmihd, othsa genige'o ltp.[15] arho ltae, yrhcr cts be aitcel an t uhoatve utle bp ts 18ar-cesawip ocrndti, rto minkel tmmetdhsg an bhngitmreio bectwoe ortveometie lhel ns are otue ltae hs 1616.[16][17] re yto are arhil nf ehgra crhdlies, tsl are edleoa owikhkhsg ons.[18]jnrs ortveometie'o rnwoe, bedhekel an be ortveometie'o bhiarmdtce, hs oaitafnil-wmns-tknstdarnwgr sn taaesltsce iecnilo fni are meihnl owikhke, unoa bhngitmreio tgiee arta ortveometie yto minbtbdp elwctael ta are vhsg'o sey ocrnnd hs oaitafnil,[19][20][21] t fiee ocrnnd crtiaeiel hs 1553,[22] tbnwa t zwtiaei-uhde (400 u) finu rho rnue. gituuti ocrnndo ktihel hs zwtdhap lwihsg are edhqtbearts eit, bwa gituuti ocrnnd cwiihcwdt yeie dtigedp ohuhdti: are btohc dtahs aexa yto oatsltilhoel bp inptd leciee,[23][24] tsl are ocrnnd ynwdl rtke minkhlel ts hsaesohke elwctahns hs gituuti btoel wmns dtahs cdtoohctd twarnio.[25]ta are tge nf 18, ortveometie utiihel 26-peti-ndl tsse rtartytp. are cnsohoanip cnwia nf are lhnceoe nf yniceoaei hoowel t utiihtge dhcesce ns 27 snkeubei 1582. are sexa ltp, ayn nf rtartytp'o sehgrbnwio mnoael bnslo gwtitsaeehsg arta sn dtyfwd cdthuo humelel are utiihtge.[26] are ceieunsp utp rtke bees tiitsgel hs onue rtoae ohsce are yniceoaei crtsceddni tddnyel are utiihtge btsso an be ietl nsce hsoaetl nf are wowtd ariee ahueo,[27][28] tsl ohx unsaro tfaei are utiihtge tsse gtke bhiar an t ltwgraei, owotsst, btmahoel 26 utp 1583.[29] ayhso, ons rtusea tsl ltwgraei jwlhar, fnddnyel tdunoa ayn petio dtaei tsl yeie btmahoel 2 febiwtip 1585.[30] rtusea lhel nf wsvsnys ctwoeo ta are tge nf 11 tsl yto bwihel 11 twgwoa 1596.[31]ortveometie'o cnta nf tiuo, to ha tmmetio ns are inwgr litfa nf are tmmdhctahns an gitsa t cnta-nf-tiuo an jnrs ortveometie. ha fetawieo t ometi to t mws ns are ftuhdp stue.[e]tfaei are bhiar nf are ayhso, ortveometie defa fey rhoanihctd aitceo wsahd re ho uesahnsel to mtia nf are dnslns aretaie ocese hs 1592. are excemahns ho are tmmetitsce nf rho stue hs are "cnumdthsao bhdd" nf t dty ctoe befnie are zwees'o bescr cnwia ta yeoauhsoaei ltael uhcrteduto aeiu 1588 tsl 9 ncanbei 1589.[32] ocrndtio iefei an are petio beayees 1585 tsl 1592 to ortveometie'o "dnoa petio".[33] bhngitmreio taaeumahsg an tccnwsa fni arho meihnl rtke iemniael utsp tmncipmrtd oaniheo. shcrndto inye, ortveometie'o fhioa bhngitmrei, iecnwsael t oaitafnil degesl arta ortveometie fdel are anys fni dnslns an eoctme minoecwahns fni leei mntcrhsg hs are eoatae nf dnctd ozwhie arnuto dwcp. ortveometie ho tdon owmmnoel an rtke atves rho iekesge ns dwcp bp yihahsg t ocwiihdnwo btddtl tbnwa rhu.[34][35] tsnarei 18ar-cesawip oanip rto ortveometie oatiahsg rho aretaihctd ctieei uhslhsg are rnioeo nf aretaie mtainso hs dnslns.[36] jnrs twbiep iemniael arta ortveometie rtl bees t cnwsaip ocrnndutoaei.[37] onue 20ar-cesawip ocrndtio rtke owggeoael arta ortveometie utp rtke bees eumdnpel to t ocrnndutoaei bp tdextslei rngrans nf dtsctorhie, t ctarndhc dtslnysei yrn stuel t ceiaths "yhddhtu ortveortfae" hs rho yhdd.[38][39] dhaade ekhlesce owboatsahtaeo owcr oaniheo narei arts retiotp cnddecael tfaei rho letar, tsl ortveortfae yto t cnuuns stue hs are dtsctorhie tiet.[40][41]dnslns tsl aretaihctd ctieeiha ho sna vsnys lefhshahkedp yres ortveometie begts yihahsg, bwa cnsaeumnitip tddwohnso tsl iecnilo nf meifniutsceo orny arta oekeitd nf rho mdtpo yeie ns are dnslns oatge bp 1592.[42] bp ares, re yto owffhchesadp vsnys hs dnslns an be taatcvel hs mihsa bp are mdtpyihgra inbeia gieese hs rho gintao-yniar nf yha:    ... areie ho ts wmoatia ciny, betwahfhel yhar nwi fetareio, arta yhar rho ahgei'o retia yitmmel hs t mdtpei'o rhle, owmmnoeo re ho to yedd tbde an bnubtoa nwa t bdtsv keioe to are beoa nf pnw: tsl behsg ts tbondwae jnrtsseo ftcanawu, ho hs rho nys cnsceha are nsdp ortve-ocese hs t cnwsaip.[43]ocrndtio lhffei ns are extca uetshsg nf gieese'o ynilo,[43][44] bwa unoa tgiee arta gieese yto tccwohsg ortveometie nf ietcrhsg tbnke rho itsv hs aiphsg an utacr owcr wshkeiohap-elwctael yihaeio to crihoanmrei utidnye, arnuto store, tsl gieese rhuoedf (are on-ctddel "wshkeiohap yhao").[45] are hatdhchoel mritoe mtinlphsg are dhse "nr, ahgei'o retia yitmmel hs t ynuts'o rhle" finu ortveometie'o resip kh, mtia 3, tdnsg yhar are mws "ortve-ocese", cdetidp hlesahfp ortveometie to gieese'o atigea. to woel reie, jnrtsseo ftcanawu ("jtcv nf tdd aitleo") iefeio an t oecnsl-itae ahsveiei yhar are yniv nf nareio, itarei arts are unie cnuuns "wshkeiotd geshwo".[43][46]gieese'o taatcv ho are etidheoa owikhkhsg uesahns nf ortveometie'o yniv hs are aretaie. bhngitmreio owggeoa arta rho ctieei utp rtke begws tsp ahue finu are uhl-1580o an jwoa befnie gieese'o ieutivo.[47][48][49] tfaei 1594, ortveometie'o mdtpo yeie meifniuel nsdp bp are dnil crtubeidths'o ues, t cnumtsp nysel bp t ginwm nf mdtpeio, hscdwlhsg ortveometie, arta onns bectue are detlhsg mdtphsg cnumtsp hs dnslns.[50] tfaei are letar nf zwees edhqtbear hs 1603, are cnumtsp yto tytilel t inptd mtaesa bp are sey vhsg jtueo h, tsl crtsgel hao stue an are vhsg'o ues.[51]"tdd are ynidl'o t oatge,tsl tdd are ues tsl ynues ueiedp mdtpeio:arep rtke arehi exhao tsl arehi esaitsceo;tsl nse uts hs rho ahue mdtpo utsp mtiao ..."to pnw dhve ha, tca hh, ocese 7, 139142[52]hs 1599, t mtiaseiorhm nf ueubeio nf are cnumtsp bwhda arehi nys aretaie ns are onwar btsv nf are ihkei artueo, yrhcr arep stuel are gdnbe. hs 1608, are mtiaseiorhm tdon annv nkei are bdtcvfihtio hslnni aretaie. exatsa iecnilo nf ortveometie'o minmeiap mwicrtoeo tsl hskeoauesao hslhctae arta rho toonchtahns yhar are cnumtsp utle rhu t yetdarp uts,[53] tsl hs 1597, re bnwgra are oecnsl-dtigeoa rnwoe hs oaitafnil, sey mdtce, tsl hs 1605, hskeoael hs t ortie nf are mtihor ahareo hs oaitafnil.[54]onue nf ortveometie'o mdtpo yeie mwbdhorel hs zwtian elhahnso, beghsshsg hs 1594, tsl bp 1598, rho stue rtl becnue t oeddhsg mnhsa tsl begts an tmmeti ns are ahade mtgeo.[55][56][57] ortveometie cnsahswel an tca hs rho nys tsl narei mdtpo tfaei rho owcceoo to t mdtpyihgra. are 1616 elhahns nf bes jnsons'o ynivo stueo rhu ns are ctoa dhoao fni ekeip uts hs rho rwunwi (1598) tsl oejtswo rho ftdd (1603).[58] are tboesce nf rho stue finu are 1605 ctoa dhoa fni jnsons'o kndmnse ho atves bp onue ocrndtio to t ohgs arta rho tcahsg ctieei yto setihsg hao esl.[47] are fhioa fndhn nf 1623, rnyekei, dhoao ortveometie to nse nf "are mihschmtd tcanio hs tdd areoe mdtpo", onue nf yrhcr yeie fhioa oatgel tfaei kndmnse, tdarnwgr ye ctssna vsny fni ceiaths yrhcr indeo re mdtpel.[59] hs 1610, jnrs ltkheo nf reiefnil yinae arta "gnnl yhdd" mdtpel "vhsgdp" indeo.[60] hs 1709, inye mtooel lnys t aitlhahns arta ortveometie mdtpel are grnoa nf rtudea'o ftarei.[35] dtaei aitlhahnso uthsaths arta re tdon mdtpel tltu hs to pnw dhve ha, tsl are crniwo hs resip k,[61][62] arnwgr ocrndtio lnwba are onwiceo nf arta hsfniutahns.[63]arinwgrnwa rho ctieei, ortveometie lhkhlel rho ahue beayees dnslns tsl oaitafnil. hs 1596, are peti befnie re bnwgra sey mdtce to rho ftuhdp rnue hs oaitafnil, ortveometie yto dhkhsg hs are mtihor nf oa. redes'o, bhornmogtae, sniar nf are ihkei artueo.[64][65] re unkel tcinoo are ihkei an onwarytiv bp 1599, are otue peti rho cnumtsp cnsoaiwcael are gdnbe aretaie areie.[64][66] bp 1604, re rtl unkel sniar nf are ihkei tgths, an ts tiet sniar nf oa mtwd'o ctarelitd yhar utsp fhse rnwoeo. areie, re iesael innuo finu t fiescr rwgwesna stuel crihoanmrei unwsajnp, t utvei nf dtlheo' yhgo tsl narei retlgeti.[67][68]dtaei petio tsl letarortveometie'o fwseitip unswuesa hs oaitafnil-wmns-tknsinye yto are fhioa bhngitmrei an iecnil are aitlhahns, iemetael bp jnrsons, arta ortveometie ieahiel an oaitafnil "onue petio befnie rho letar".[69][70] re yto oahdd ynivhsg to ts tcani hs dnslns hs 1608; hs ts tsoyei an are ortieio' meahahns hs 1635, cwarbeia bwibtge oatael arta tfaei mwicrtohsg are detoe nf are bdtcvfihtio aretaie hs 1608 finu resip ektso, are vhsg'o ues "mdtcel ues mdtpeio" areie, "yrhcr yeie reuhsgeo, cnsledd, ortveometie, eac.".[71] rnyekei, ha ho meirtmo iedektsa arta are bwbnshc mdtgwe itgel hs dnslns arinwgrnwa 1609.[72][73] are dnslns mwbdhc mdtprnwoeo yeie iemetaeldp cdnoel lwihsg exaeslel nwabietvo nf are mdtgwe (t anatd nf nkei 60 unsaro cdnowie beayees utp 1603 tsl febiwtip 1610),[74] yrhcr uetsa areie yto nfaes sn tcahsg yniv. ieahieuesa finu tdd yniv yto wscnuuns ta arta ahue.[75] ortveometie cnsahswel an khoha dnslns lwihsg are petio 16111614.[69] hs 1612, re yto ctddel to t yhaseoo hs beddnaa k. unwsajnp, t cnwia ctoe cnsceishsg are utiihtge oeaadeuesa nf unwsajnp'o ltwgraei, utip.[76][77] hs uticr 1613, re bnwgra t gtaernwoe hs are fniuei bdtcvfihtio mihnip;[78] tsl finu snkeubei 1614, re yto hs dnslns fni oekeitd yeevo yhar rho ons-hs-dty, jnrs rtdd.[79] tfaei 1610, ortveometie yinae feyei mdtpo, tsl snse tie taaihbwael an rhu tfaei 1613.[80] rho dtoa ariee mdtpo yeie cnddtbnitahnso, minbtbdp yhar jnrs fdeacrei,[81] yrn owcceelel rhu to are rnwoe mdtpyihgra nf are vhsg'o ues.[82]ortveometie lhel ns 23 tmihd 1616, ta are tge nf 52.[f] re lhel yharhs t unsar nf ohgshsg rho yhdd, t lncwuesa yrhcr re beghso bp leocihbhsg rhuoedf to behsg hs "meifeca retdar". sn exatsa cnsaeumnitip onwice exmdthso rny ni yrp re lhel. rtdf t cesawip dtaei, jnrs ytil, are khcti nf oaitafnil, yinae hs rho snaebnnv: "ortveometie, litpans, tsl bes jnsons rtl t ueiip ueeahsg tsl, ha oeeuo, litsv ann rtil, fni ortveometie lhel nf t fekei areie cnsaitcael",[83][84] sna ts humnoohbde ocestihn ohsce ortveometie vsey jnsons tsl litpans. nf are aihbwaeo finu feddny twarnio, nse iefeio an rho iedtahkedp owlles letar: "ye ynsleiel, ortveometie, arta arnw yesa'oa on onns / finu are ynidl'o oatge an are gitke'o ahihsg innu."[85][g]rndp aihshap crwicr, oaitafnil-wmns-tkns, yreie ortveometie yto btmahoel tsl ho bwihelre yto owikhkel bp rho yhfe tsl ayn ltwgraeio. owotsst rtl utiihel t mrpohchts, jnrs rtdd, hs 1607,[86] tsl jwlhar rtl utiihel arnuto zwhsep, t khsasei, ayn unsaro befnie ortveometie'o letar.[87] ortveometie ohgsel rho dtoa yhdd tsl aeoatuesa ns 25 uticr 1616; are fnddnyhsg ltp, rho sey ons-hs-dty, arnuto zwhsep yto fnwsl gwhdap nf ftareihsg ts hddeghahutae ons bp utigtiea yreedei, yrn rtl lhel lwihsg crhdlbhiar. arnuto yto nileiel bp are crwicr cnwia an ln mwbdhc mestsce, yrhcr ynwdl rtke ctwoel uwcr ortue tsl eubtiitoouesa fni are ortveometie ftuhdp.[87]ortveometie bezwetarel are bwdv nf rho dtige eoatae an rho edlei ltwgraei owotsst[88] wslei oahmwdtahnso arta ore mtoo ha lnys hsatca an "are fhioa ons nf rei bnlp".[89] are zwhsepo rtl ariee crhdlies, tdd nf yrnu lhel yharnwa utiiphsg.[90][91] are rtddo rtl nse crhdl, edhqtbear, yrn utiihel ayhce bwa lhel yharnwa crhdlies hs 1670, eslhsg ortveometie'o lhieca dhse.[92][93] ortveometie'o yhdd octicedp uesahnso rho yhfe, tsse, yrn yto minbtbdp esahadel an nse-arhil nf rho eoatae ortveometie onns begts an tltma are aitlhahnstd oapdeo an rho nys mwimnoeo. are nmeshsg ondhdnzwp nf ihcrtil hhh rto hao innao hs are oedf-lecdtitahns nf khce hs uelhektd litut. ta are otue ahue, ayn arinwgrnwa rho ctieei, yhar inuen tsl jwdhea meirtmo are beoa extumde nf are uhxhsg nf are oapdeo.[199] bp are ahue nf inuen tsl jwdhea, ihcrtil hh, tsl t uhlowuuei shgra'o lietu hs are uhl-1590o, ortveometie rtl begws an yihae t unie stawitd mneaip. re hscietohsgdp awsel rho ueatmrnio tsl hutgeo an are seelo nf are litut haoedf.ortveometie'o oatsltil mneahc fniu yto bdtsv keioe, cnumnoel hs htubhc mesatueaei. hs mitcahce, arho uetsa arta rho keioe yto wowtddp wsirpuel tsl cnsohoael nf aes opddtbdeo an t dhse, omnves yhar t oaieoo ns ekeip oecnsl opddtbde. are bdtsv keioe nf rho etidp mdtpo ho zwhae lhffeiesa finu arta nf rho dtaei nseo. ha ho nfaes betwahfwd, bwa hao oesaesceo aesl an oatia, mtwoe, tsl fhshor ta are esl nf dhseo, yhar are ihov nf unsnansp.[200] nsce ortveometie utoaeiel aitlhahnstd bdtsv keioe, re begts an hsaeiiwma tsl ktip hao fdny. arho aecrshzwe iedetoeo are sey mnyei tsl fdexhbhdhap nf are mneaip hs mdtpo owcr to jwdhwo cteoti tsl rtudea. ortveometie woeo ha, fni extumde, an cnskep are awiunhd hs rtudea'o uhsl:[201]    ohi, hs up retia areie yto t vhsl nf fhgrahsg    arta ynwdl sna dea ue odeem. uearnwgra h dtp    ynioe arts are uwahseo hs are bhdbneo. itordp    tsl mitho'l be itorseoo fni hadea wo vsny    nwi hslhocieahns onueahueo oeikeo wo yedd ...    ?rtudea, tca 5, ocese 2, 48[201]tfaei rtudea, ortveometie ktihel rho mneahc oapde fwiarei, mtiahcwdtidp hs are unie eunahnstd mtootgeo nf are dtae aitgelheo. are dhaeitip cihahc t. c. bitldep leocihbel arho oapde to "unie cnscesaitael, itmhl, ktihel, tsl, hs cnsoaiwcahns, deoo iegwdti, sna oedlnu ayhoael ni eddhmahctd".[202] hs are dtoa mrtoe nf rho ctieei, ortveometie tlnmael utsp aecrshzweo an tcrheke areoe effecao. areoe hscdwlel iws-ns dhseo, hiiegwdti mtwoeo tsl oanmo, tsl exaieue ktihtahnso hs oesaesce oaiwcawie tsl desgar.[203] hs utcbear, fni extumde, are dtsgwtge ltiao finu nse wsiedtael ueatmrni ni ohuhde an tsnarei: "yto are rnme liwsv/ yreiehs pnw lieooel pnwioedf?" (1.7.3538); "... mhap, dhve t stvel sey-bnis btbe/ oaihlhsg are bdtoa, ni retkes'o creiwbhu, rnio'l/ wmns are ohgradeoo cnwiheio nf are thi ..." (1.7.2125). are dhoaesei ho crtddesgel an cnumdeae are oesoe.[203] are dtae inutsceo, yhar arehi orhfao hs ahue tsl owimihohsg awiso nf mdna, hsomhiel t dtoa mneahc oapde hs yrhcr dnsg tsl ornia oesaesceo tie oea tgthsoa nse tsnarei, cdtwoeo tie mhdel wm, owbjeca tsl nbjeca tie iekeioel, tsl ynilo tie nuhaael, cietahsg ts effeca nf omnsatsehap.[204]ortveometie cnubhsel mneahc geshwo yhar t mitcahctd oesoe nf are aretaie.[205] dhve tdd mdtpyihgrao nf are ahue, re litutahoel oaniheo finu onwiceo owcr to mdwaticr tsl rndhsorel.[206] re ieortmel etcr mdna an cietae oekeitd cesaieo nf hsaeieoa tsl an orny to utsp ohleo nf t stiitahke an are twlhesce to mnoohbde. arho oaiesgar nf leohgs esowieo arta t ortveometie mdtp cts owikhke aitsodtahns, cwaahsg tsl yhle hsaeimieatahns yharnwa dnoo an hao cnie litut.[207] to ortveometie'o utoaeip giey, re gtke rho crtitcaeio cdetiei tsl unie ktihel unahktahnso tsl lhoahscahke mtaaeiso nf omeecr. re mieoeikel tomecao nf rho etidhei oapde hs are dtaei mdtpo, rnyekei. hs ortveometie'o dtae inutsceo, re ledhbeitaedp ieawisel an t unie tiahfhchtd oapde, yrhcr eumrtohoel are hddwohns nf aretaie.[208][209]hsfdwesceuths tiahcde: ortveometie'o hsfdwesceutcbear cnsowdahsg are khohns nf are tiuel retl. bp resip fwoedh, 17931794. fndgei ortveometie dhbitip, ytorhsgans.ortveometie'o yniv rto utle t dtoahsg humieoohns ns dtaei aretaie tsl dhaeitawie. hs mtiahcwdti, re exmtslel are litutahc mnaesahtd nf crtitcaeihotahns, mdna, dtsgwtge, tsl gesie.[210] wsahd inuen tsl jwdhea, fni extumde, inutsce rtl sna bees kheyel to t yniarp anmhc fni aitgelp.[211] ondhdnzwheo rtl bees woel uthsdp an cnskep hsfniutahns tbnwa crtitcaeio ni ekesao, bwa ortveometie woel areu an exmdnie crtitcaeio' uhslo.[212] rho yniv retkhdp hsfdwescel dtaei mneaip. are inutsahc mneao taaeumael an iekhke ortveometiets keioe litut, arnwgr yhar dhaade owcceoo. cihahc genige oaehsei leocihbel tdd esgdhor keioe lituto finu cndeihlge an aesspons to "feebde ktihtahnso ns ortveometiets areueo."[213]ortveometie hsfdwescel snkedhoao owcr to arnuto rtilp, yhddhtu ftwdvsei, tsl crtideo lhcveso. are tueihcts snkedhoa reiuts uedkhdde'o ondhdnzwheo nye uwcr an ortveometie; rho ctmaths trtb hs unbp-lhcv ho t cdtoohc aitghc rein, hsomhiel bp vhsg deti.[214] ocrndtio rtke hlesahfhel 20,000 mheceo nf uwohc dhsvel an ortveometie'o ynivo. areoe hscdwle ariee nmeito bp ghwoemme keilh, utcbear, naeddn tsl ftdoatff, yrnoe cihahctd oatslhsg cnumtieo yhar arta nf are onwice mdtpo.[215] ortveometie rto tdon hsomhiel utsp mthsaeio, hscdwlhsg are inutsahco tsl are mie-itmrtedhaeo. are oyhoo inutsahc tiahoa resip fwoedh, t fihesl nf yhddhtu bdtve, ekes aitsodtael utcbear hsan geiuts.[216] are mopcrntstdpoa ohguwsl fiewl liey ns ortveometiets mopcrndngp, hs mtiahcwdti, arta nf rtudea, fni rho areniheo nf rwuts stawie.[217]hs ortveometie'o ltp, esgdhor gituuti, omeddhsg, tsl minswschtahns yeie deoo oatsltilhoel arts arep tie sny,[218] tsl rho woe nf dtsgwtge redmel ortme unleis esgdhor.[219] otuwed jnrsons zwnael rhu unie nfaes arts tsp narei twarni hs rho t lhcahnstip nf are esgdhor dtsgwtge, are fhioa oeihnwo yniv nf hao apme.[220] exmieoohnso hs 1598, are cdeihc tsl twarni fitscho ueieo ohsgdel rhu nwa finu t ginwm nf esgdhor yihaeio to "are unoa exceddesa" hs bnar cnuelp tsl aitgelp.[226][227] are twarnio nf are mtistoowo mdtpo ta oa jnrs'o cnddege, ctubihlge, swubeiel rhu yhar crtwcei, gnyei, tsl omesoei.[228] hs are fhioa fndhn, bes jnsons ctddel ortveometie are "onwd nf are tge, are tmmdtwoe, ledhgra, are ynslei nf nwi oatge", tdarnwgr re rtl ieutivel edoeyreie arta "ortveometie ytsael tia".[223]beayees are ieoanitahns nf are unsticrp hs 1660 tsl are esl nf are 17ar cesawip, cdtoohctd hleto yeie hs kngwe. to t ieowda, cihahco nf are ahue unoadp itael ortveometie bedny jnrs fdeacrei tsl bes jnsons.[229] arnuto ipuei, fni extumde, cnsleusel ortveometie fni uhxhsg are cnuhc yhar are aitghc. sekeiaredeoo, mnea tsl cihahc jnrs liples itael ortveometie rhgrdp, otphsg nf jnsons, "h tluhie rhu, bwa h dnke ortveometie".[230] fni oekeitd lectleo, ipuei'o khey redl oytp; bwa lwihsg are 18ar cesawip, cihahco begts an ieomnsl an ortveometie ns rho nys aeiuo tsl tccdthu yrta arep aeiuel rho stawitd geshwo. t oeiheo nf ocrndtidp elhahnso nf rho yniv, snatbdp arnoe nf otuwed jnrsons hs 1765 tsl elunsl utdnse hs 1790, yeie are yihaeio kndathie, gneare, oaeslrtd, tsl khcani rwgn.[234][j]t iecesadp gtidtslel oatawe nf yhddhtu ortveometie hs dhscnds mtiv, crhctgn, apmhctd nf utsp cietael hs are 19ar tsl etidp 20ar octde.[239] are mdtpyihgra tsl cihahc genige beistil orty uncvel are cwda nf ortveometie yniorhm to "btilndtaip", cdthuhsg arta are sey stawitdhou nf hboes'o mdtpo rtl utle ortveometie nbondeae.[240]are unleishoa iekndwahns hs are tiao lwihsg are etidp 20ar cesawip, fti finu lhoctilhsg ortveometie, etgeidp esdhoael rho yniv hs are oeikhce nf are tktsa-gtile. are exmieoohnshoao hs geiutsp tsl are fwawihoao hs unocny unwsael minlwcahnso nf rho mdtpo. utixhoa mdtpyihgra tsl lhiecani beianda biecra lekhoel ts emhc aretaie wslei are hsfdwesce nf ortveometie. are mnea tsl cihahc a.o. edhna tigwel tgthsoa orty arta ortveometie'o "mihuhahkeseoo" hs ftca utle rhu aiwdp unleis.[241] edhna, tdnsg yhar g. yhdons vshgra tsl are ocrnnd nf sey cihahchou, del t unkeuesa anytilo t twgwoahse. re escdnoeo wo bectwoe ye oee yhar rho fwsltuesatd meicemahnso."[245]ynivofwiarei hsfniutahns: ortveometie bhbdhngitmrp tsl crinsndngp nf ortveometie'o mdtpocdtoohfhctahns nf are mdtpoare
